Important Dispatches

128th Meeting of the Legislative Yuan 71

The Legislative Yuan held its 128th meeting at 8:00 a.m. on the 24th. The committee members present were Luo Ding, Shi Shangkuan, Lu Zhonglin, Zhao Shibei, Liu Kejun, Zhu Luhe, Li Shuhua, Zhu Hezhong, Xi Chaojun, Liu Jingxin, Peng Yangguang, Lu Zhiyi, Lin Bin, Chen Changheng, Shi Weihuan, Fang Juehui, Wu Tiecheng, Wei Huai, Liu Shishun, Sun Jingya, Cai Kun, Feng Zhaoyi, Dai Xiujun, Zhang Mojun, Huang Shichang, Niu Yongjian, Ma Chaojun, Zhou Wei, Jiao Yitang, Ma Yinchu, Wei Tingsheng, Lou Tongsun, Wang Yongbin, Wang Baozhen, Liu Jixue, Zhu Jingsong, Zhuang Songfu, and Chairman Hu Hanmin. The matters for discussion were as follows: (1) Review of the Draft Organization Law of the Administrative Court. It was resolved to refer it to the Legislative Committee for review. (2) Report from the Legislative Committee of the Yuan: Review of the Draft Amendments to the Organization Regulations of the Huai River Commission. It was resolved to pass it with amendments. (3) Report from the Self-Government Law Drafting Committee of the Yuan: Re-examining and amending the provision in Article 7, Paragraph 2 of the County Organization Law that neither townships nor towns shall exceed one thousand households, and whether it can be changed. After reviewing the results, it was considered that there are clear provisions in Article 7, Paragraph 2 of the revised County Organization Law, and it is not appropriate to change it. If the townships and towns have been compiled before the amendment of this law, they will be allowed to maintain their current status. It was resolved to retain it. (4) Report from the Self-Government Law Drafting Committee of the Yuan: Review of the Executive Yuan's request for interpretation of various points of doubt in the City Organization Law. After reviewing the results, they were divided into three points for interpretation. First, the district-fang self-government convention, the district affairs meeting, the fang affairs meeting, and the district mediation committee have no clear provisions. Because they are not needed, there are no provisions. Second, although the election of neighborhood chiefs and ward chiefs and the number of attendees are not detailed, they can be handled in accordance with the provisions of Articles 122 and 137 of the law. Third, prostitutes are an improper business and violate national laws, so they cannot be recognized as citizens. It was resolved to retain it. (5) Amendment to the Village Clearing Regulations. It was resolved to refer it to the Legislative and Military Committees for review. (6) Report from the Legislative Committee of the Yuan jointly with the Labor Law Drafting Committee: Review of the Implementation Law of the Farmers' Association. It was resolved to pass it with amendments. (7) Deliberation on the Draft Code of Civil Procedure, Book 5, Chapter 4, Personal Litigation Procedure. It was resolved to leave it for discussion at the next meeting.

Legislative Yuan Amends the Organizational Regulations of the Huai River Commission 72

The Legislative Yuan held its 128th meeting on the morning of the 24th and passed the amended Organizational Regulations of the Huai River Commission as follows: (Article 1) The Huai River Commission is directly under the National Government and is in charge of all matters related to the management and treatment of the Huai River. (Article 2) The administrative agencies and stationed troops in the Huai River basin have the responsibility to provide assistance and protection when the Commission performs its duties. (Article 3) The Commission shall notify the land administration agencies to handle the land exposed as a result of the management and treatment of the Huai River. (Article 4) The Commission shall have a Chairman and Vice Chairman each appointed by the National Government, and a number of committee members, and shall designate five standing committee members from among the committee members to preside over the affairs of the Commission. (Article 5) The Commission shall hold a standing committee meeting once a month and a plenary committee meeting once every three months, and may convene extraordinary meetings when necessary. (Article 6) The implementation of the resolutions of the Commission and the handling of internal affairs shall be carried out in the name of the Chairman. (Article 7) The Commission shall have an Engineering Department and a Secretariat. (Article 8) The Engineering Department shall be responsible for the following matters: 1. Matters relating to investigation and surveying; 2. Matters relating to engineering design; 3. Matters relating to the implementation and maintenance of engineering; 4. Matters relating to engineering examination; 5. Matters relating to the custody of materials and tools; 6. All other engineering matters. (Article 9) The Secretariat shall be responsible for the following matters: 1. Matters relating to documents, statistics, and their custody; 2. Matters relating to the registration of appointment and dismissal of staff; 3. Matters relating to accounting; 4. Matters relating to the formulation and preparation of budgets and final accounts; 5. Matters relating to general affairs and maintenance; 6. Matters relating to the reporting of exposed land; 7. Matters relating to the custody of seals; 8. Other matters not belonging to the Engineering Department. (Article 10) The Engineering Department shall have a Chief Engineer, a Deputy Chief Engineer, one or two persons, and four to six Chief Engineers appointed by the Commission. Engineers, Deputy Engineers, Assistant Engineers, administrative staff, workers, and clerks shall be appointed by the Commission. (Article 11) The Secretariat shall have a Director, who shall be appointed to a senior-level position, three or four section chiefs, who shall be appointed to a recommended-level position, and twenty to twenty-four staff members, who shall be appointed to a delegated-level position. (Article 12) The Commission may hire engineering experts as consultants or members. (Article 13) The Commission may employ employees as necessary for its affairs. (Article 14) This law shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Wuhan Garrison to Convene Another Conference on Pacification in Three Provinces 73

He Chengjun to Return to Hankou to Supervise Bandit Suppression

Hankou Correspondence: Since the Wuhan Garrison convened a pacification conference regarding military bandit suppression in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, the armies of the three provinces have, according to plan, launched offensives on multiple fronts, eliminating many bandits over the past two months. However, on the 31st of last month, the 18th Division suffered a setback at Donggumen, causing bandit forces to reignite. Additionally, remnants of He and Kuang's bandit gangs in the border areas of Hunan and Hubei have taken the opportunity to cause disturbances. Those concerned about the bandit scourge in the three provinces are worried. Fortunately, Honghu, which had long been occupied by bandits, was captured by troops of the 10th Army, severing connections for He and Kuang's bandit forces. The armies of Sichuan, Hubei, and Hunan were then able to encircle them. Furthermore, the Wugong Mountains on the borders of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi were destroyed by troops of the 9th Army, resulting in the on-site killing of several bandit leaders. Although the communist bandits in Jiangxi are relatively rampant, their connections with the bandits in Hunan and Hubei have been severed, and their strength has been greatly diminished after fierce battles with the 18th Division. If attacked again by crack troops, they can be wiped out in one fell swoop. He Chengjun, head of the Wuhan Garrison, in order to thoroughly eliminate the communist bandits, traveled from Hankou to Nanjing to pay respects to Commander-in-Chief Chiang, personally reporting on the situation of bandit suppression in the three provinces. He also indicated that since a garrison was also established in Nanchang, its scope of authority needed to be clarified with Commander-in-Chief Chiang. It is reported that after arriving in Nanjing, He, along with Tu Jin Yu, the superintendent for bandit suppression and rural pacification on the borders of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, and Xia Douyin, the commander of the 21st Route Army, visited Chiang for several days, consulting on the outcome. Commander-in-Chief Chiang greatly appreciated He's new plan for bandit suppression and instructed He in person that all matters related to bandit suppression in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi should still be under the full command of the Wuhan Garrison, assigning him sole responsibility. After receiving the order, He plans to stay in Nanjing for a few more days before returning to Hankou to preside over affairs. Given that the strength of bandit forces in the three provinces changes daily, the methods of advancement and suppression must be carefully considered. He plans to convene another conference on pacification in the three provinces immediately after returning to Hankou, gathering the commanding officers of the bandit suppression forces from the three provinces, the chiefs of staff of each army, division, and brigade, personally inquiring about the latest bandit suppression situation, and providing instructions on new strategies. The period for complete suppression will still be in accordance with the deadline set by Commander-in-Chief Chiang: March 31st. Those who have not been completely suppressed by then will be punished. As for bandit suppression expenses, in Jiangxi Province, in addition to the original troops being paid by the provincial government, the remaining national army will be paid directly by the central government. In Hunan Province, because there are fewer guest troops, it is also easier to raise funds. However, in Hubei Province, after the downsizing, finances are extremely difficult, and there are several times more national troops stationed in Hubei than in Hunan. Previously, the provincial government decided to issue 3 million yuan in bandit suppression bonds, later renamed as post-war recovery bonds. The issuance regulations have been approved by the Ministry of Finance. The bonds are denominated in 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, 10 yuan, and 5 yuan denominations, and are allocated to each county and city in the province. The Wuhan Banking Group is provisionally allocated 800,000 yuan, the two Wuhan business associations 500,000 yuan, the provincial government 300,000 yuan, each county 100,000 yuan, each city and town 270,000 yuan, and the remainder is allocated from Wuhan rental income. The funds raised from the issuance of these bonds will be used for bandit suppression expenses. (January 22nd)

Recent News on Bandit Suppression Divisions in Jiangxi Province 74

The 18th and 50th Divisions to Undergo Streamlining

Han Deqin Has Led His Division Headquarters to Nanchang

Nanchang Correspondence: Commander-in-Chief Chiang issued a clear order to temporarily postpone the streamlining of all bandit suppression units. However, the 18th and 50th Divisions suffered significant casualties in the recent bandit suppression campaigns in Longgang, Dongshao, and Zhongcun. They returned to the rear for reorganization and replenishment, hence taking this opportunity to undertake streamlining. It is learned that Tan Daoyuan's 50th Division had long received orders to be streamlined into a Class B division. This month, Division Commander Tan ordered his troops to gradually move from Yihuang and Bingfeng to Zhangshu to concentrate. The division was streamlined into two brigades with six regiments. Except for the 150th Brigade under Luo Shouyi, which was disbanded, the 148th Brigade under Cheng Guangyao and the 149th Brigade under Yue Sen (concurrently Deputy Division Commander) retained their original regimental, battalion, and company commanders, only changing their numbers. After the streamlining of the division is completed, they will intensify training in Zhangshu and request the central government to send personnel for inspection. After the inspection, they will advance to the front to suppress bandits. As for the 18th Division, it also received orders to reorganize according to the Class B division system, eliminating half. Except for Zhu Yaohua's 54th Brigade, which is still suppressing bandits at the front, the 52nd and 53rd Brigades have moved to Fengcheng Qingjiang to reorganize. It is reported that Acting Division Commander Xiao Wenduo has completed the reorganization of his unit according to the Class B system. The 53rd Brigade was disbanded, and the 105th and 106th Regiments under that brigade were incorporated into the 101st and 102nd Regiments of the 52nd Brigade, with Dai Yue and Zhu Yaohua continuing to serve as brigade commanders. Many lower-ranking officers have been transferred and replaced, and requests for replenishment of firearms have been submitted to the headquarters.

After arriving in Nanchang, Han Deqin's 52nd Division moved to the upper reaches of the Gan River. Division Commander Han Deqin, along with Deputy Division Commander Tu and Chief of Staff Luo, led the division headquarters and directly subordinate units from Xun to the province on the evening of the 20th. The division headquarters was set up at the Gao Sheng Lane Law and Politics Special School. On the afternoon of the 22nd, the provincial government hosted a banquet at the West Flower Hall to welcome Han and other senior officers, expressing their appreciation. It is heard that Han will soon lead his division headquarters to the upper reaches of the Gan River, commanding his troops to strive for the complete elimination of communist bandits. (January 22nd)

Communist Bandits Occupy Huarong Three Times 75

Changsha Correspondence: Since He Long fled from western Hubei into western Hunan, only three months have passed, but he has repeatedly harassed the counties of Nanhua, Jinshi, Li, and Lin in Hunan, and Gongshi and Songhe in Hubei. Huarong County has fallen twice. In the middle of last month, Li Ming, the brigade commander of the 32nd Brigade of the 11th Division, rushed from Yuezhou to recover it. In the period of a little over a month, although Li's brigade recovered the county seat of Huarong, the four rural areas of Huarong have become bandit-controlled. Duan Dechang's force of 3,000 to 4,000 communist bandits has dispersed and remained hidden in the villages and lakes of Shizui and Diaoxian in Huarong. Recently, Li's brigade received orders from Division Commander Chen Cheng to return to Yuezhou for reorganization. According to the central government's designated area-based bandit suppression plan, it should have been taken over by Xiao Zhichu's 44th Division. However, because Xiao's division was still suppressing bandits in southern Hubei, it was unable to arrive immediately. Zeng Jingshan, the magistrate of Huarong County, repeatedly telegraphed the province, reporting the rampant bandit situation and requesting that Li's brigade be temporarily stationed. If Li's brigade could not stay in the county and Xiao's division could not take over, he requested that Division Commander Li Jue of the 19th Division send troops to take over to avoid negligence. Unexpectedly, Li's brigade, eager to reorganize, completely withdrew to Yuezhou on the 16th. Li's division was also suppressing He Long in the Lizhou area and could not dispatch troops to Huarong for relief. The county seat was empty, and the county magistrate, being timid, dared not stay and left the city with the troops on the 16th, temporarily moving the county government to Beijinggang. Before leaving, he sent a telegram saying: "The troops stationed in the county were completely withdrawn this morning. The relief troops are not expected to arrive. The public is panic-stricken, and order is disrupted. An emergency meeting was called, and it was unanimously stated that the defense is empty, the bandit situation is vast, and it is difficult to resist with the remaining local defense forces with limited ammunition. It is advisable to temporarily retreat to Beijinggang for office work. Although I have a responsibility to defend the territory, I am helpless. I have no choice but to follow the public opinion. Once the troops have completely withdrawn, I will order the local defense forces to concentrate, on the one hand, supporting the people to evacuate to safety, and on the other hand, supervising the teams to block and intercept. In case of a disparity in strength, I will retreat again. I implore you to quickly order Division Commander Li Jue to dispatch troops for assistance, which may provide some remedy. Otherwise, Huarong will fall for the third time, and the people will suffer unimaginable hardships. I urgently submit my words, filled with anxiety and awaiting orders. Zeng Jingshan, the magistrate of Huarong County, bows." Upon receiving the report, He Jian immediately telegraphed the two divisions of Li Jue and Zhang Ying, ordering them to quickly dispatch troops for assistance. However, it was too late. Duan Dechang led his troops to attack in three directions on the afternoon of the 16th and arrived at the county seat of Huarong early on the 17th. At that time, the troops and local defense forces had already retreated completely. Duan's bandits captured it effortlessly. The third fall of Huarong has shaken Nanxian and Yuanjiang, which have telegraphed the province for emergency assistance. The telegram from Nanxian stated: "Li's brigade in Huarong emptied the defense on the day before yesterday and was captured at dawn. The affiliated counties are in imminent danger. In addition to working with the military to do our best to block, we urgently request the dispatch of a large army for assistance to save the crisis. Tan Renwei, the magistrate of Nanxian, bows." The telegram from Yuanjiang stated: "According to reports, the majority of Duan's bandits launched a three-pronged attack on Huarong at noon the day before yesterday and captured the county seat at dawn. Lianyu Wharf has also fallen. Magistrate Zeng retreated with the 11th Division to Yueyang. The bandits have reached Shakou. The local defense forces of Huarong have retreated to the Wupo Diaoyuzui area. The garrison in Nanxian is guarding the county river mouth five miles from the county seat of Nanxian. The affiliated counties have dispatched teams to block the area near Babai Gong. Please quickly send a large army for assistance and suppression. Fang Xin, the magistrate of Yuanjiang, bows."

It is heard that after occupying Huarong on the 17th, Duan's bandits launched a three-pronged attack on Nanxian on the 19th. Fortunately, Zhang Ying's Sichuan army had dispatched two regiments, Duan and Zhou, to block the river at Hongyangzha, so the bandits failed to cross the river. In addition, Division Commander Li Jue also dispatched two regiments for assistance, requiring them to concentrate in Nanhua before the 21st. Once the assembly is complete, they will launch a general attack on Huarong. According to He Jian's report at the provincial government memorial week on the 19th, he stated that the county could be recovered soon. However, the people have once again suffered devastation. (January 20th)

Key Hunan Communist Leader Yang Youlin Captured 76

Changsha Correspondence: Yang Youlin, a key communist leader in Hunan Province, was originally a middle school student from Xiangxiang County. In 1924, he joined the Communist Party and implemented communist work. In 1926, when the Communist Party was in power in Hunan, Yang served as a member of the Provincial Farmers' Association Executive Committee, manipulating the provincial farmers' movement, organizing peasant self-defense forces, instigating riots, confiscating property, and brutally killing countless innocent people. In 1927, after the May Incident, Yang fled to the Ping-Liu area with Yi Lirong and Dai Yuan, disappearing without a trace. On July 27th of last year, when the communist bandit Peng Dehuai captured Changsha, Yang returned to the province and served as a member of the puppet Soviet Hunan Provincial Government, issuing orders and directing riots. Because Yang had lived in the province for a long time, he was very familiar with the situation in Changsha. He knew which families were well-off and which were wealthy merchants, and he assigned red bandits to capture, kill, loot, and plunder. Even middle-class families suffered greatly, so the citizens of Changsha hate Yang to the bone. After the recovery of the provincial capital, Yang also fled without a trace. Unexpectedly, he recently returned to his hometown in Xiangxiang with orders from the Communist Party, preparing to mobilize the local defense forces and ignorant people in Xiangxiang to join the Communist Party and take the opportunity to create chaos. Fortunately, the Xiangxiang County neighborhood watch forces detected this and secretly dispatched 20 soldiers on the evening of the 18th to surround Yang's residence, capturing him on the spot. They also found plans and resolutions for communist sabotage in Hunan in his home. Yang was handed over to the Xiangxiang County Government. County Magistrate Tian Jifeng proposed a strict interrogation. Yang denied being Yang Youlin, claiming that his name was Yang Zailin and that he was Yang Youlin's cousin, merely living in the same house. However, many people in Xiangxiang confirmed that he was definitely Yang Youlin and requested his execution to prevent him from escaping justice. Upon receiving the report, He Jian ordered the Xiangxiang County Government to hand over Yang to the provincial government for interrogation soon. (January 20th)

Yang Shuzhuang Returns to Fujian from Shanghai 77

Immediately Convening Provincial Committee to Discuss Military and Post-War Matters

Fuzhou Correspondence: Yang Shuzhuang, chairman of the provincial government, recently went to Nanjing upon orders. Now, because the financial problems of Fujian Province have been discussed and a solution has been found, and the provincial situation urgently needs to be resolved, he returned to Fujian on the 18th from Shanghai aboard the Pu'an transport ship with Zheng Baoqing, Yang Sui, Wu Shu, and Shi Jialin. He entered the port on the morning of the 20th and returned to the provincial government in the afternoon. Yang's return to Fujian has four major tasks: (1) strengthening the provincial government organization; (2) reorganizing local finances; (3) eliminating communist bandits on the Fujian border; and (4) reorganizing the provincial defense forces. On the 21st, Yang convened a temporary meeting of the provincial government committee. Regarding military and post-war matters, it was decided to abolish the Temporary Military Affairs Office and establish a Security Office, with Fang Shengtao as the director. All provincial defense forces, provincial police, guerrilla teams, and advance teams will be handed over to this office for reorganization. Fang has scheduled to go to southern Fujian within a week to inspect the troops of Chen Guohui, Gao Jingli, Liang Jichuan, and Huang Bingwu, and to divide the defense areas. After the procedures are completed, he will return to the province to organize the Security Office. Furthermore, the temporary meeting of the provincial government decided that the three units currently stationed in northern Fujian, Liu Heding's division, Zhou Ziqun's brigade, and Zhang Ziming's brigade, will be ordered to move to Jiangxi Province to join the Sixth Route Army in attacking communist bandits. Currently, the vanguard unit of Liu Shangzhi's brigade of Liu's division has arrived in Ningdu on the Jiangxi border. The two brigades of Chen Wantai and Gui Zhenyuan are also advancing towards Jiangle Guihua Jianning. Zhou Ziqun's brigade has arrived in Ninghua on the Fujian border, and Zhang Ziming's brigade has also arrived in Tai Ning on the Fujian border. They are expected to all enter Jiangxi within ten days. Liu Heding telegraphed the provincial government, reporting the situation of departure and requesting the dispatch of troops to take over defense in the counties on the Fujian border. The provincial government also decided to order the three brigade units of Lu Xingbang, Qian Yuguang, and Lin Bingzhou, currently stationed in Yongan Jianyang Jianou, to be responsible for deployment. Regarding financial issues, it was decided to implement a business tax to supplement funds. Once the Ministry of Finance issues the tax regulations, the Finance Department will prepare to implement it. (January 21st)

Shanxi Province Starts Downsizing 79

All to Be Completed by the End of This Month

Taiyuan Correspondence: Since receiving the downsizing order, Shanxi Province has had the Department of Finance and the Likin Tax Office consult and, starting from January 1st, first abolished the three locations of the Shuohuguan, PingSui Railway Joint Collection Bureau, and ZhengTai Railway Train Goods Donation Bureau. The Sai Bei matters are within the scope of Suiyuan Province and are being handled by the Suiyuan Provincial Government. The Shuohuguan and other places are currently being closed down and are expected to be completely abolished by the end of this month. As for the various consolidated tax bureaus under the province, Minister of Finance Qiu Zengyi and Shang Qiyu recently agreed in Tianjin to abolish them immediately. The Department of Finance has received a telegram from Qiu ordering the immediate transfer of the order to the various bureaus, limiting the collection of taxes to stop uniformly from the 20th of this month, and requiring all the work to be completed by the end of this month. All salaries of all bureau staff will be paid until the end of this month. It is learned that there are a total of twenty-one consolidated tax bureaus in the province (namely Cheguan, Bailan, Xiaguan, Dayou, Hebao, Xingyukou, Xueqi, Yushuan Ferry, Miaowu, Xiamakou, Fenglingdu, Maojin Ferry, Gaoluo, Lanjun, Dahekou, Dongyanggouan, Malinguan, Liaoxian, Nichengkou, Huaiwei, etc.). Second Trial of the Judge Ha Murder Case 81

Victim Zhang Wang Liqing Appears in Court

Testimony Offering Exoneration for Ye Yixiong

Harbin Dispatch: The case of Ye Yixiong shooting his mistress Zhang Wang Liqing continued its hearing at the Binjiang Court this afternoon (19th) at 2:30 PM. Since the last public hearing, the public's interest in this case has only grown. Dozens have gone to the court daily to seek to continue hearing the trial. Yesterday, news of the continued hearing was received, and knowing that the female protagonist Zhang Wang Liqing was determined to appear, driven by curiosity, everyone hurried to attend the hearing. By 11:00 AM, many people were arriving one after another. Fearing rejection by the court, many pretended to be journalists. By 2:00 PM, more than a hundred men and women had arrived. The court specially opened a large living room to accommodate the audience as a temporary resting room. Court President Guo Yilin stated that the number of attendees broke the court's existing record. He bustled about in the courtroom, directing bailiffs and arranging seats. The first criminal court was larger, so it was converted into a courtroom, but ultimately, due to the small room and many people, there were only forty seats in the audience, requiring much arrangement. The trial was originally scheduled to begin at 2:00 PM, but due to the victim Zhang Wang Liqing's absence, it was delayed until 2:35 PM. Zhang Wang Liqing arrived at the court by car at 2:25 PM, accompanied by her lawyer, Chi Long. When Zhang alighted from the car, the audience crowded into the courtyard to see her. Those who did not get a good look followed her to the bailiff's room where she was resting, peering through the doorway to catch a glimpse. Zhang wore a blue satin fox fur-trimmed cape, a yellow felt hat, and blue velvet boots. She walked with light, healthy steps, displaying a composed demeanor. However, her face still showed signs of illness. When the trial began at 2:35 PM, the audience rushed to their seats. Those who were quick managed to secure seats, while those who could not find seats crowded at the doorway, clamoring incessantly. In the end, the court president had no choice but to make a special concession, allowing dozens of audience members to ascend the platform and stand next to the judge's bench, resembling the constables in the old-fashioned yamen. After the trial began, many people continued to arrive, knocking on the courtroom door and begging to be let in. Several bailiffs stood inside and outside the door, strictly preventing unauthorized entry. Therefore, the sounds of knocking and arguing were constantly heard. Those who could not enter the courtroom could only gaze longingly at the doorway and sigh. However, many did not want to make the trip in vain, enduring the cold and standing in the courtyard, waiting for a glimpse of Zhang Wang Liqing's face. Only after the court was adjourned and Zhang Wang Liqing left the court with her lawyer did the crowd disperse. It is rumored that this case will have a third trial in a week, after all the witnesses have been summoned. Because Ye and Zhang's testimonies have been repeatedly reversed, whether Ye is guilty depends on the witnesses' testimonies at the next trial. The details of today's trial are recorded as follows:

First, Ye Yixiong was questioned. Ye originally had shackles on his feet. The court, seeing that there were too many audience members, which was unseemly, temporarily removed the restraints. Judge (Question): Ye Yixiong, when did you buy your handgun? Ye (Answer): Winter of the 11th year. I don't remember the date. I was studying at the Russian school at the time. My classmate surnamed Rui knows about it. (Question): Where did you buy it? (Answer): At the gun shop on 14th Street of China Avenue. (Question): Did you obtain a gun license? (Answer): I had one before. (Question): Where is the gun license now? (Answer): I don't remember. It's been eight or nine years, and I have two homes, so I don't know where it is. (Question): Do you remember the gun license number? (Answer): The number has too many digits. I don't remember it now. (Question): You said your classmate surnamed Rui knows about the gun purchase. What is his name? (Answer): Rui Youban. We are old classmates and have been friends for seven years. (Question): What is his occupation? (Answer): Formerly the section chief of the Education Department. (Question): Is it the Education Department of the Special District? (Answer): Yes. (Question): Where does he live? (Answer): I don't remember his address. When my lawyer meets with me, I can ask him to inquire. Also, last time I didn't have time to say many things. Please allow me to speak, Judge. When I was at Shuangcheng Station, all the paper and the chop were not searched out. At that time, there was a patrol chief and two policemen in the room. I took them out myself and handed them over. (Question): You can't remember your gun license number. After you shot her, where did you throw the gun? (Answer): After the incident, I ran to the side. When I fell, the snow was very deep, and the gun fell into the snow. Because the snow was very deep, I couldn't find it. I didn't throw it. (Question): Your original statement said that after you committed the murder, you didn't walk far. There was a small grove, resembling a park. The snow was very deep, and you threw the gun there. How can you say it fell? (Answer): I didn't throw it. It fell. (Question): After firing a shot, did you search her body? Did you find anything? (Answer): The snow was very deep. I was only concerned with running. She was crying and shouting. How could I dare search her? (Question): The remittance of 7,050 yuan, remitted from your hand to Beiping, who would pick it up in Beiping? (Answer): It wasn't decided. There are many procedures for withdrawing the money. (Question): Do you need a guarantor to withdraw the money in Beiping? Is it paid without a guarantor, or is it withdrawn with a stamp? (Answer): I don't know the details. You'll only know when you withdraw the money in Beiping. (Question): When will you know? (Answer): I don't know about the money. (Question): On the 23rd, where did you travel to by train? You needed the key to open the box before you saw the letter with the mooncake drawing? (Answer): At the time, I didn't know where I was going, because it was too hot inside the train. I was wearing two pairs of woolen trousers, which was too much. I wanted to change trousers, but since I didn't bring any luggage, I planned to take one pair off and put it in Ms. Zhang's box. Just then, Ms. Zhang wanted a cigarette and gave me the key. Why didn't I change my trousers? Because when I opened the box, I saw the letter and got angry and didn't change them. Last time, the judge asked if I cried or cursed. I really didn't. And there are many things that happened that I didn't say last time because I was short on time. Please allow me to recount them. At the time, after I saw the letter, I was very angry. I thought, unless I give her a shot, or she gives me a shot, that's the end of it. So, the more I thought about it, the angrier I got, seeing that letter from her giving Ke Long a drawing. Of course, she was going to Beiping to marry him. Before long, the train station arrived. At this time, I thought, if she goes to Beiping, I really don't want her to. How can I stop her from going? So, I said that there are good views in this place, tricking her into getting off the train. Actually, the train stopped for seven minutes. I said sixty minutes. After getting off the train, we walked west away from the station. As we walked, Ms. Zhang said she was afraid of bandits and wasn't satisfied with me. I thought, forget it. We've had a good relationship for over a year. I can't bear to hurt her. But I also wanted to persuade her to return to Harbin, but she didn't want to. So, I was very sad. As we walked, the train left. Ms. Zhang saw the train leaving and was even more unwilling. So, she grumbled. As we got close to the warehouse, her voice grew louder, and she began to quarrel. I thought, she's even more set on that thing in the letter. At this time, Ms. Zhang cursed me, "You're nothing. Who would want to go with you?" I said, "Good sister, you decide. You don't want to go with me. Do you want to go with Liu Ke Long?" She said, "I'll go with Liu Ke Long. It's none of your business." As we walked, Ms. Zhang slipped on the snow and fell. At this time, I was very angry and gave her a shot. I didn't expect it to happen. I really didn't expect that ten years of studying, my entire career, and reputation would be lost. As Ye recounted to this point, his voice was faint and filled with sorrow. His eyes were full of tears. The judge then said, (Question): Ye Yixiong, what you just said contradicts what you said last time, that you tricked Zhang Liqing off the train and walked past the water building, from the first warehouse to the second warehouse, across the light rail, to Shouzi Tomb, saying that the road was difficult to walk. You even helped Zhang Liqing walk, and she was crying and cursing, but you were smiling and saying, "Good sister, let's go." Today, you say you were pondering this and pondering that, starting to want to kill her, then not wanting to kill her, and finally killing her. According to you,

Page 12

Today, you also say that Zhang wanted to marry Liu Ke Long, the letter had a mooncake on it, inviting him to eat mooncakes, and she cursed you, which made you angry enough to kill her. What you have said today contradicts what you said last time. You know that changing your story only makes things worse. It's better to just be direct and tell the truth. (Answer): What I said last time was because I had been detained for dozens of days. It's been a long time, and I didn't think of everything. Actually, that's how the event unfolded. (Question): When you opened the box to see the letter, where had the train travelled to? How far was it from Shuangcheng? (Answer): At first, I didn't know where we were going. As we walked, the train slowed down, and I knew we were arriving at a station. (Question): Exactly how much time passed between opening the box and arriving at Shuangcheng? (Answer): Not much time. (Question): Three or four minutes? (Answer): I don't remember. (Question): What was written in that mooncake letter? (Answer): A mess. I couldn't see it clearly. I couldn't remember everything. There were words like "The Mid-Autumn Festival has arrived. Please eat a mooncake." Underneath, there was a drawing of a mooncake. Next to it, it was written, "This mooncake is almost to your mouth." Underneath, it was written, "Want to be with you..." dots. (Question): How many letters did you see before you saw this letter? (Answer): I just flipped through them. When I saw that this letter was important, I looked at it. (Question): Did you not see anything else? (Answer): There were also family letters, for Zhang's family. There were many. Because they were family letters, it is not good to read other people's letters, so I didn't read them. There were many other letters. I don't remember them. (Question): What did the letter you said you saw say? (Answer): It said, "The Mid-Autumn Festival has arrived. Please eat a mooncake." I don't remember the details. (Question): How many pages was that letter? (Answer): I don't remember. The mooncake in the letter was drawn on the left side of one page, near the end of where it was written. I don't know how many pages. (Question): Did you read the entire letter? (Answer): I skimmed it. (Question): What kind of pen was it written with? (Answer): It was probably written with a fountain pen. I don't remember. (Question): After you opened the box, did you return the key? (Answer): After opening the box, I hung the key there. Ms. Zhang came in at this time. I quickly closed it and took the key, putting it casually in my pocket. I was wearing a Zhongshan suit with four pockets. I casually put it down. I felt very ashamed for reading other people's letters. Ms. Zhang saw that my complexion was not good, so she left. (Question): After you shot her, did you touch anything on her body? (Answer): I didn't touch anything. I was already feeling bad, and I was in a hurry. How could I touch her body? (Question): According to what you say, after you shot her, you hid away, and you didn't touch anything on her body. (Answer): She was yelling and screaming. How could I touch anything? The judge ordered Zhang Wang Liqing to be brought in. (To be continued)

Difficult to Abolish Additional Tax on Anhui Salt 82

Provincial Defense Military Expenses Have No Way to Be Subsidized

The financial difficulties of Anhui Province have a long history. After the separation of the Provincial Finance Department and the Special Finance Office last year, the Likin tax was allocated as central revenue. The provincial treasury only relied on the land and head tax and miscellaneous taxes of various counties for subsidies, and the shortfall between income and expenditure has increased significantly. This time, the abolition of the Likin tax has been particularly exhausting. The provincial government decided to levy an additional tax on salt per jin, 2.4 yuan per shi, as compensation. Recently, the Ministry of Finance, based on petitions from the people of 21 counties in northern Anhui, telegraphed the provincial government to abolish this additional tax. The provincial government stated that the provincial defense military expenses relied on this subsidy and that there were no other funds to raise. Yesterday, it specially replied to the Ministry of Finance, detailing the difficult situation, stating that the Ministry had approved a cable stating that the Bengbu Huai Salt Merchants Association and other groups, as well as the representatives of the people of 21 counties in northern Anhui, including Peng Zhuoru, had telegraphed one after another, stating that the provincial government had set up bureaus in Bengbu and Tunxi, adding additional taxes on salt, requesting a prompt telegram to stop them. The cable also instructed to follow the previous cable to abolish them. This case had previously been approved by the Ministry's 30th cable, stating that Anhui citizen Li Yongbin and others had telegraphed the same situation, instructing that it be abolished. It had already been consulted and replied to the government. The provincial government believes that Anhui's finances are at their extreme. All situations are well known to the Ministry. Currently, the provincial defense military expenses are more than 2.7 million yuan, and there is really no way to subsidize them. There is absolutely no other way to compensate except by promoting the additional tax on salt. Anhui Province obeys the central government's orders and does not dare to have its own separate policies. The difficult situation and expedient measures must also be understood by the Ministry. In the future, when the communist bandits are eliminated and the local area is peaceful, this additional tax should be abolished at any time. As for the issue of smuggled salt being flooded in, both northern and southern Anhui have special smuggling bureaus, and inspections are very serious. There is no need to worry about it being flooded in and circumventing. The previous reasons for the cable, in addition to having been submitted to the Executive Yuan for filing, are appropriately consulted and replied to, and request review.

Jiangsu Province Prepares for Spring Afforestation 83

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines has designated the anniversary of the death of Dr. Sun Yat-sen on March 12th of this year as the date for tree planting. At that time, the afforestation movement should be carried out in accordance with the order, which will benefit the forestry industry. Therefore, the "General Outline of the Afforestation Movement Plan for Each County in Jiangsu Province for the Year 20" has been specially formulated, and it was issued to the county governments yesterday, requiring them to prepare a plan and submit it for approval within 20 days of receiving the document. The outline is recorded below:

(1) Organization: The county government and the county party department are responsible for convening various agencies, mass organizations, and schools to organize an afforestation movement committee, which should be divided into general affairs, publicity, tree planting, and other groups.

(2) Location: Select locations according to the following principles: (1) Convenient transportation, (2) Easy management, (3) Suitable soil, (4) Beneficial to scenery, (5) Beneficial to hygiene.

(3) Area: For afforestation movement expenses less than 500 yuan, the planting area is 15 mu to 30 mu; less than 1,000 yuan, 30 mu to 50 mu; less than 1,500 yuan, 50 mu to 120 mu; for those exceeding 1,500 yuan, the area should be appropriately increased according to this ratio.

(4) Seedlings: Select seedlings according to the following principles: (1) Suitable for wind and soil, (2) Healthy growth, (3) Wide range of uses, (4) Beautiful posture, (5) Long life. The types of seedlings to be used must be listed and submitted for approval in advance. The table should be divided into nine columns: name, number of plants, rows, area, seedling height, price per hundred seedlings, total seedling price, source of seedlings, and remarks. The total number should be listed after the table for assessment.

(5) Number of plants: For afforestation movement expenses less than 500 yuan, plant 3,000 to 5,000 plants; less than 1,000 yuan, plant 5,000 to 10,000 plants; less than 1,500 yuan, plant 10,000 to 20,000 plants; for those exceeding 1,500 yuan, the number of plants should be appropriately increased according to this ratio. (The above refers to the number of plants to be planted at the planting site, and the number of plants to be promoted is outside.)

(6) Charts: Draw a rough map of the planting site, using a scale of 1/1000, but a small area can use 1/500, and a large area can use 1/2000. The table must be concise and complete. (7) Expenses: In accordance with the finalized plan, 5% of the agricultural and forestry business income of each county will be used as a special fund for the afforestation movement, and the expenses will be based on the approved budget. If there is no county-level agricultural and forestry business income, the county government shall be responsible for quickly raising funds and preparing a budget for approval.

(8) Ceremony: For the ceremony, a stage must be set up in advance at the venue, planting pits must be dug in advance, and the planting area must be delineated according to the number of participants from each group. After gathering at the ceremony venue and performing the ceremony, form a procession to parade.

(9) Publicity: Promote as much as possible with reference to the following methods: A. Written publicity: Compile three types of slogans, leaflets, and pamphlets, using simple text and pictures to express them. B. Oral publicity: Divided into speeches at the planting site, parades and speeches in urban and rural areas, and masquerade speeches.

(10) Protection: The county government where the planting site is located shall issue a notice to the public, and the Public Security Bureau, the county-run agricultural, forestry, and sericulture farms, and the district offices, village heads, security corps, and public security sub-bureaus that have jurisdiction over the area shall be responsible for proper protection and management, and shall patrol and replant at any time to ensure that the forest is thriving. If it is necessary to set up a forest guard post, it may be applied for approval and set up to protect it. (24th)

Local Correspondence

Nanhui 84

Accused of Theft, Suicide Saved: Zhang Yixian, a farmer in Huinong Township in the county, had his fence destroyed by thieves the other night, who entered and stole items. When this was discovered, the security corps of the township was notified and arrested the thief. The township head, Gu Xiuzhang, interrogated him. According to his confession, his name was Cao Laosan, a native of the township, and he falsely accused Chen Yezi from the neighboring township (West Seventh Township) of being a lookout. The township head immediately arrested Chen Yezi, forced him to write a letter of repentance, and demanded 27 yuan to avoid prosecution. Although Chen Xiangsheng testified that Chen Yezi had always been law-abiding, it was to no avail. Under the pressure of accumulated authority, Chen had no choice but to reluctantly agree. However, he later realized that he was greatly humiliated and had no face to show anyone. So, last night, he obtained several doses of opium and swallowed them in an attempt to commit suicide. Fortunately, he was discovered by villagers, who treated him in various ways and saved him from danger.

Water Police Cracked Many Theft Cases: The Fourth Brigade of the Water Police Provincial Public Security Team stationed in Datuan has recently been dispatching police to investigate bandit traces due to the winter defense emergency. A few days ago, they arrested Song Tanggui and his brother A Shu at Shenjia Pier. Tanggui confessed to repeatedly committing robbery cases and admitted to robbing Tang Songlin's family recently. Xu Miaoquan was also arrested at Central Bridge, who confessed to joining Shen Ayou and others in robbing Deng Tailai's store at Xuanjia Bridge and joining the Communist Party. It is reported that these bandits have now been sent to the Nanhui County Government for prosecution.

Songjiang 85

Education Bureau Abolishes Lunar New Year and Conducts Inspections of Schools: The Education Bureau previously decided at a bureau affairs meeting to abolish Lunar New Year and communicated this to all schools and social education institutions, ordering that no holidays be granted. Fearing that the order would be obeyed superficially but violated in reality, the 66th bureau affairs meeting stipulated that personnel would be sent to investigate in three districts from February 13th to 27th, inspecting no less than one-third of the schools. Those who did not comply with the law would be severely punished. Hu's Wife Murder Case Court Hearing Record: Hu Yinglong of Da Wuqiao was prosecuted for the murder of his wife, and his stepmother, Hu Nie, was prosecuted for assisting in the murder. The Criminal Court of the court held a public trial on the afternoon of the 22nd. This case attracted much attention, and the audience was very crowded, making it impossible to conduct the trial. Therefore, the court dismissed the corpse brother Zhang Zeqian and others and rescheduled the hearing for 9:00 AM this morning (24th). Criminal Court Judge Li and Prosecutor Ren and Secretary Li took their seats in the courtroom. The defendant's lawyers Zhang Baopei and Gu Shouyi, the witnesses Zhang Shaoxiu, physician, Tao, forensic examiner, and Zhu, as well as the plaintiff and defendant, were all present awaiting trial. The audience was still very crowded, but the order was good. After the informer Zhang Zeqian made his statement, the forensic examiner Tao was questioned, who stated that the examination of the corpse revealed finger marks on the neck, so it was determined that it was a strangulation injury. Lawyers Zhang and Gu selectively questioned this. Then, Dr. Zhang Shaoxiu made a statement (Dr. Zhang was hired by the informer to inspect the scene), saying that the death was caused by suffocation, and there was much debate. Later, Zhu Qia'an testified that Hu Yinglong had suffered from neurasthenia since childhood and had always been well-behaved, so he would not have caused this tragedy. At this point in the questioning, it was past noon, and the judge ordered a 40-minute recess, and then continued the questioning at 8:00 PM in the evening.

Suzhou 86

Five Children Kidnapped in Zhouzhuang Township: In Guojia Dian, Zhouzhuang Town in the county, the home of villager Xu Zhaolin was suddenly broken into by more than a dozen bandits at around 1:00 AM yesterday, who kidnapped three of Xu's sons and one son and one grandson of neighbor Shen Kunxiang. The team leader Yang immediately led a team to pursue them, but the bandits had already travelled far.

Tragic Boat Capsizing in Baiyang Bay: Qian Husheng and his younger brother Baosheng, along with their 12-year-old son, were returning to their village from the city by boat on the night before last (23rd). Also on board was Li Wu, a 65-year-old neighbor. As they sailed about two or three li from Tiger Hill into Baiyang Bay Lake, a sudden gale arose, and it was dark. There was no response to their cries for help, causing the boat to capsize. All four people on board drowned. Yesterday, Li Wu's son Tianbao and Husheng's mother Lu arrived at the scene to recover the bodies and filed a report with the District Attorney's Office to allow them to be taken away without examination.

Bandits Rampant Between Suzhou and Wujiang: In Xinta near Luhu in Wujiang County, five or six large bandit ships were discovered the night before last (23rd). The number of people was unknown due to the darkness. Upon receiving the report, the Third District of the Suzhou Water Police immediately dispatched the warships Peirong and Anjing, led by District Chief Shen Gaochan, as well as several teacher ships, to suppress them at 2:00 AM yesterday (24th). At the same time, it was reported that 50 or 60 bandit ships were discovered at Langda Temple in Dangjiao, the border between Suzhou and Changshu. Shen sent the first squad of the eleventh team, together with Yang Qingjiu, the team leader of the thirteenth team stationed in Changshu, to suppress them. Also, at Chenhua Wharf in Chefang, Suzhou Township, four bandit ships carrying more than a hundred bandits arrived at 10:00 AM yesterday (24th) and kidnapped Zhou Banghua, a clerk from the Xiangchun Nanhuo store in the town. The security corps of Chefang, Jiaozhi, and Xietang joined forces to pursue them. Upon hearing the news, Team Leader Pei of the Eleventh Water Police Team continued to assist in the suppression. Also, at Guojia Dian in Zhouzhuang, one bandit ship arrived at 2:00 AM yesterday (24th) and kidnapped three sons of villager Xu Zhaolin and one son and one grandson of Shen Kunxiang, heading towards Taihu Lake. The county government dispatched a police team to pursue and rescue the hostages.

Wuxi 87

Shanghai Kidnappers Capture Famous Kidnapper Shen Xiaohuzi (Jiangbei Native): Shen Xiaohuzi, who had been colluding with others to kidnap and extort huge sums of money in the Shanghai area, recently fled to Wuxi, hiding near the Student Silk Factory outside Guangfu Gate on Dongxin Road. The Shanghai Special City Public Security Bureau learned of this and immediately dispatched detectives to Wuxi yesterday to cooperate with the county police team in the arrest. They captured the bandit Shen Xiaohuzi (the suspect is only in his twenties) in a teahouse next to the Housheng Silk Factory. The team temporarily detained him, awaiting official documents to be sent to Wuxi for his case to be heard and dealt with.

Liyang: Robbery and Disturbances in Townships: Since Liyang suffered successive bandit attacks the year before last, the government has taken strict precautions, and the villagers have become like startled birds. Late one night, more than ten bandits suddenly appeared in Qilicun, a place seven miles outside the north gate. Each carried firearms and planned to rob the village's residents. They first entered a certain family's home and only managed to rob several dozen silver dollars and a few gold rings. Just as they were about to continue robbing another family, a neighbor sounded the alarm. Soon, nearby militia and police teams rushed to surround and capture the bandits, who then fled with their stolen goods. The urban public security bureau also received the news, but without knowing the true situation, immediately dispatched police to the countryside to encircle and capture them. The city gates were immediately closed, and travelers passing through were strictly interrogated. After about two hours, things returned to normal. At that time, a steamship from Wuxi to Liyang had arrived in the wilderness about ten miles from the city. Receiving the alarm and faintly hearing gunfire, it stopped proceeding. Only after learning that the bandits had disappeared did it start sailing to Liyang, but the passengers had already suffered a scare. Furthermore, Zhuxiang reported another robbery case. Zhu Xinsan, a resident of Zhangjing Bridge Lane in the Seventh District of Huai’an, owned a modest amount of farmland. His son, Shuigen, is currently a teacher at a university in Shanghai. Recently, Zhu Xinsan built six or seven new-style Western-style houses next to his old house, which unfortunately attracted the attention of bandits. At around ten o'clock on the night before last, four robbers, speaking with northern accents and wielding weapons, suddenly arrived, opened the gate, and one bandit stood guard outside while three bandits entered to rob. Zhu Xinsan, seeing the bandits coming to rob, immediately escaped through the back door. His wife, née Bao, came out to negotiate with the bandits and handed over 227 silver dollars. The bandits, not satisfied with what they received, then arbitrarily searched the room of Zhu's wife, née Bao. After about an hour, they left with their stolen goods. In this incident, a total of three gold rings, one pair of gold bracelets, one gold lock pendant, one gold chain, and silver ornaments and clothing were robbed, with a total loss of more than 700 dollars.

Changshu 88

Four Families Robbed in One Night in the Seventh District: Nanhudang in the Seventh District of this county, with its branching harbors, also borders Wuxi. On the night of the 21st, four families were robbed in the Lijiajiao area of Liulitang. It is reported that the bandits numbered about twenty to forty people. After landing from Huadang, they first went to the home of Wei Genggen in Jixiang of Ximajing, Liulitang, and broke into the house. They first fired two shots from a local musket, and then beat anyone they encountered. Genggen's mother, née Xu, was injured by the bandits with wooden sticks, and the hairpins on her bun were also snatched away. Genggen was forced to hand over silver dollars but could not produce them, and was also tortured and bruised. As a result, more than twenty piculs of white rice, more than ten chickens, more than fifty silver dollars, and jewelry, totaling about more than 400 dollars, were robbed. After the robbery, they went to the homes of Li Jinfu, Li Guangen, and Li Tongtong in Lijiajiao to rob, resulting in the theft of silver dollars, white rice, clothing, etc., totaling about more than 600 dollars. Then, they wandered around Tangbei, shining electric torches brightly. The villagers sounded the alarm, but the bandits still did not retreat. Later, they fired several shots before scattering. According to subsequent speculation, there may be clues to this robbery. Several peddlers from Jiangbei selling small books and dredging river mud arrived in the town last month, which is quite suspicious.

Kun-Chang Early Steamship to Resume Service Soon: Due to a dispute over route rights between the Huitong Company and the Tai Dong Lou Qin Chang Qing Joint Company regarding the additional Kun-Chang early steamship service, both sides suspended service pending resolution. Now, upon receiving an order from the department, the three joint companies, not having registered, were specifically ordered to suspend the Kun-Chang route, allowing the Huitong Bureau to operate the route. Orders have already been issued to both Kunshan and Changshu counties to comply. It is expected that the Kun-Chang early steamship service will resume soon.

Jiangyin 89

Investigation of the Military and Police of Wujin Entering the Territory to Suppress Bandits: Due to the expansion of bandit forces in the northern countryside of Wujin County (bordering Jiangyin), the police team and thirty to forty members of the Big Knife Team from Shangxu Village gathered in the Yuantong Nunnery in Qiujiatou, Jiangyin County, the other day, capturing more than ten bandits and beheading Chen Songlin. Cao Zongduo, the head of the Sixth District, reported the situation to the county. Magistrate Li ordered Yin Geng, the head of the Sixth Branch of Public Security, to go to investigate. Yin arrived at Yuantong Nunnery and questioned Huang Gengmei, who claimed that on the afternoon of the 15th of this month, at 7 p.m., two or three people came to the temple to burn incense, followed by more than ten people who also came to burn incense. Suddenly, gunshots were heard outside the nunnery, and members of the Big Knife Team and county police entered, arresting more than ten people and beheading one. The deceased was named Chen Songlin, a native of Wujin, with injuries on his hands and feet. Chen had served as a detective for the Longhutang Security Team in Wujin and was known to be restless. The fourteen people arrested were also not good people. Huang also stated that he was not a member of the temple staff, but a carpenter, and that a member of the temple staff had been stabbed three times and was unable to come to the bureau. After questioning, Huang was to be sent to the county for further questioning.

Zhenjiang 90

Strict Punishment for Dishonest Public Servants: The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs recently approved an official letter from Cao Minghuan, a member of the Jiangsu Provincial Party Affairs Consolidation Committee, stating that according to comrades from Tonghai and other counties, dishonest district chiefs and security team leaders in Nantong, Haimen, Rugao, Taixing, Jingjiang, and other places often extorted money from good citizens in the name of eliminating reactionaries, accusing them of being communists, releasing them after receiving bribes, and killing those who did not pay. Furthermore, when genuine communist elements were captured, they were allowed to confess after receiving bribes. Such situations urgently needed to be corrected. It was requested that the provincial government strictly order the county governments to stop such unfortunate incidents from occurring. District chiefs and security team leaders, being public servants close to the people, should maintain their integrity and set an example for the people. If they were to extort money under false pretenses or engage in bribery and corruption, it would be illegal. Therefore, the provincial government yesterday specifically instructed the county magistrates to conduct thorough and secret investigations. Once verified, they should be severely punished according to the law.

Representatives of the Experimental Elementary School Teachers' Union Petition: Due to the long delay in the issuance of salaries to various schools, causing extreme hardship, the teachers and staff of the Provincial Experimental Elementary School publicly elected Chen Bangyan, Fan Ganfu, Gan Cheng, and others to jointly petition the Department of Education yesterday. Section Chief Yang of the Second Section received them. The representatives stated three points: (1) The delay in salaries has severely affected the livelihoods of colleagues; (2) The outstanding funds must be issued by the end of January; (3) The salary standards and seniority-based salary increase methods for the staff of the Experimental Elementary School urgently need to be established and revised. Section Chief Yang replied, stating that the department was aware of the hardship caused by the delay in salaries for elementary school teachers and staff and was determined to find ways to raise funds. He would send another letter to the Education Fund Management Office soon, requesting that the outstanding salaries be cleared by the end of January. As for raising salary standards and seniority-based salary increase methods, due to limited funding, it was not possible to implement them immediately. The department was determined to plan in advance in the shortest possible time and hoped to realize them within the 20th year of the Republic. The representatives considered the reply satisfactory and then took their leave.

Gaoyou 91

Anhui Bandits Besiege Longgang Town: Longgang Town in the 12th District of this county was suddenly attacked yesterday (the 21st) by hundreds of bandits who had crossed over from Anhui Province. They dispersed around the town. The garrison troops stationed in the town, being outnumbered, dared not engage in battle and are currently holding fast to the earthen walls. They have sent people to the city to request that the county government send troops to assist them as soon as possible. Magistrate Wang ordered Police Captain Mu Shidu to lead a team to suppress them this morning.

County Magistrate Robbed En Route: Wang Guanxian, the former Magistrate of Qianfu County, set off from his native Huaian with his family the other day to go to the province. However, when he arrived at a place fifteen miles south of Fanshui in Baoying County, he was suddenly met by more than ten bandits who shouted for him to stop and swarmed onto the boat. He was robbed of 400 dollars in cash, three boxes of clothing, and one piece of luggage. He immediately telegraphed the Department of Civil Affairs, requesting that all counties be ordered to strictly investigate.

Nantong 92

Tonghai District Sea Defense and Pacification: The Provincial Pacification Commissioner has divided the eight counties of Tonghai into one district and appointed Zhao Jianxun, the brigade commander of the 94th Brigade of the 32nd Division, as the commander. On the 23rd, Zhao's troops began to garrison various counties. Furthermore, due to the unrest caused by bandits along the coast of various counties, a joint sea defense association was established, patrol teams were organized, and shallow-water warships were purchased. A meeting will be held in Haimen within days to discuss the progress.

Organizational Structure of the Pacification Office: Military, political, and police agencies in Tong County have jointly organized a pacification office. Shi Dexue has been appointed as the director, and Zhang Dong and Wang Dechang as the deputy directors. The office has a reconnaissance team specializing in investigating bandits and communists, and a patrol team patrolling the cities and countryside. There are also trial, clearing, and propaganda sections. The required funds are to be allocated by the county government, and the office is to be dissolved in three months.

Rugao 93

Pig Merchant Dies at the Hands of Bandits on His Way Home: Gu Jiantao from Gaomingzhuang, Lugang District, obtained 180 dollars from He Jinji's pig shop in Zhanghuanggang on the first day of the lunar November, along with two copper stoves, a powder scoop, and two pieces of white cloth. He was accompanied by Yang Zong'er, the son of Shi Laizhi, on his way home. When they reached Caijiabao, Zhu Zongru, a bandit staying in a temple, led a group of bandits to rob Gu of his money and goods. They then tied him up with a rope, stabbed him three times, and he died of his injuries. Gu's son, Gu Changqing, came to the city yesterday to go to the county and requested that officials be sent to investigate.

Petition to Hold Feast and Education Donations: The Education Bureau, since the collection of sutra-chanting donations has been ordered to cease by the department, and the overdue fines must be fully remitted to the province, and since another method of compensation has been ordered by the provincial department, after investigation, Wuxi and Nantong counties have both been approved by provincial order to hold feast donations. The Education Bureau yesterday specially drafted regulations for the collection of feast education donations and submitted them to the county government for forwarding to the provincial government for approval and implementation so that education funds could be slightly supplemented.

North and South Sea Bandits Clash: Chen Dachuan from Nankan Town, Juegang, who was previously abducted by bandits and forced to work on their ship, returned after more than three months. According to him, there are currently 35 bandit ships anchored in that port, led by bandit leaders Pan Kaiwu, Song Lishan, and Zhou, with more than 1,000 coastal bandits. They have many rifles and mortars, as well as four steel cannons, two copper cannons, eight handheld machine guns, and nine large local cannons, and claim to be carrying out the extermination of the northern gang of Shen's bandits.

Sea Bandits Extort Ransom for Hostages: Three hostages were previously taken from Huoshaozha, Changsha Town, Juegang. On the 13th, the bandits sent letters to the families, demanding 500 dollars for Cao Erhou, 100 dollars for Tian Shikui, and 1,000 dollars for Gao Da, a resident of the Seventh District, claiming that the bandit ship would be sailing north soon and that the money must be prepared quickly for their ransom.

Pinghu 94

Hostages from Xindongwei Rescued: Cao Erhe's family in Xindongfang Grain Embankment, Xintai, had three women kidnapped by bandits on New Year's Eve. The bandits initially demanded 40,000 dollars, eventually reducing it to 10,000 dollars. The Cao family received the letter and entrusted someone to negotiate, first paying 7,000 dollars to redeem the three kidnapped women. With 3,000 dollars still owed, they were supposed to deliver it on the second day of the New Year. Unexpectedly, when they were delivering the money, while passing through the Ziqing Temple in Nanxiangfang, the money was robbed by another group of bandits, so they had to turn back and find another way.

Troops Go to Quangongting to Suppress Bandits: At 2:00 a.m. on the 19th, the Special Service Company of the 3rd Battalion of the 7th Regiment of the Provincial Security Team, along with a unit of the X Company stationed in Xincang, set off at 8:00 a.m. to search for bandits in Quangongting but found nothing. According to someone from Shantang Town, in the evening of the 18th, seven large bandit boats carrying sixty to seventy armed bandits, including important bandit leaders, passed through there and left the port. The boats were carrying many women, presumably those kidnapped from various villages, and seemed to have heard that troops were coming to suppress them, so they fled.

Hangzhou 95

Construction Department Dredges the Fuchun River: The Fuchun River, connecting the Qiantang River downstream and reaching Yanlan upstream, is a major waterway in eastern and western Zhejiang. Recently, due to silt deposition at Xindian Beach in the upper reaches between Changkou and Chengfen, and at Changling in the lower reaches north of Yushan, the riverbed has risen. Whenever there is drought and low water levels, shipping is greatly inconvenienced. The Construction Department yesterday ordered the Water Conservancy Bureau to plan comprehensively and schedule dredging. In addition to allocating funds from ship license tax revenue, it is also encouraging local people to donate and the Qianjiang Revitalization, Dahua, and other shipping companies to make special donations.

Yangling Fishing Terrace Petitioned for Reconstruction: The Yanling Fishing Terrace is one of the ancient sites in Zhejiang Province. Having been in disrepair for many years, it is insufficient to simply preserve it without undertaking repairs. County Magistrate Wang of Tonglu submitted a petition to the province requesting the allocation of public funds for reconstruction. The provincial government ordered the Civil and Financial Departments to deliberate and reply, stating that at present, with financial difficulties and the provincial treasury exhausted, there were no funds available to allocate and it was difficult to approve. The actual cost of the project and whether it was possible to raise funds locally for reconstruction should be determined. The county magistrate was ordered to comply yesterday.

Ningbo 96

Salt Police Intercept Large Batch of Smuggled Salt: The Ci-Xi Sanqi City Salt Police Bureau Inspection Office received a tip-off yesterday stating that a large number of salt smugglers were transporting many loads of smuggled salt and would be passing through Sanqi City. Upon receiving the tip-off, the office immediately dispatched several salt police officers to wait at Chaling Bridge. At around 11:00 p.m., they saw more than fifty salt smugglers carrying salt loads coming towards the bridge. The salt police ordered them to stop, but the salt smugglers refused, putting down their salt loads and surrounding the salt police with their carrying poles. Seeing that the situation was not good, the salt police quickly fired shots into the sky, broke through the encirclement, and escaped. Upon hearing the news, the Inspection Office immediately dispatched more salt police officers to rush over. Knowing that they could not resist, the salt smugglers abandoned the salt and fled. The police then hired boats to load the eighty to ninety bags of smuggled salt and transport them to Ningbo for disposal by the Salt Police Bureau.

Brother Mistaken for Wild Boar and Shot Dead: Ma Boyi, a farmer in Ma'ao, Taiqiu District, Zhenhai, had a passion for hunting. A few days ago, after a heavy snowfall, at around 8:00 p.m., he went up the mountain to hunt with a loaded gun. Crouching in the thorns, he soon saw a shadow crawling from afar, mistaking it for a wild boar, and fired. Suddenly, he heard a scream and, abandoning his gun, rushed to see what had happened. It was his brother, Bo Ren. Bo Ren was a businessman in Xuebo and happened to be returning home that day. Because the journey was long, it was already dark when he arrived in his hometown, leading to his being shot dead by his brother. It was both a coincidence and a tragedy.

Fengxian 97

County Government Revises Defense Zones: The most important aspect of defense in this county is the area bordering Songjiang, Shanghai, and Fengxian in the south. Therefore, County Magistrate Shen Qingkang raised the matter for discussion at the joint defense conference of the three counties. It was decided that Zhaolin, Ruanxiang, and Hujiaqiao, bordering Songjiang and Fengxian, would be patrolled by the neighboring Shanyang police team. Sili and Datuan, bordering Fengxian and Nanhui in the south, would be supported by the joint defense guerrilla team, which would install long-distance telephones. Wujiaqiao and Zhangjiatang, bordering Fengxian, Nanhui, and Songjiang, have also been designated as special areas in the winter defense conference of this county. In addition to consulting with the Minhang River Police and the joint guerrilla team to rotate troops to strengthen the force, Zhu Wenyu, the captain of the county police wooden shell gun team, has been ordered to inspect each pass with the second team at the Shazhu posts in the vicinity to ensure thoroughness.

Xiaoshan 98

Township Offices to Be Established Soon: Since County Magistrate Du of Xiaoshan received the central government's decree on the township system, he has repeatedly ordered the district offices to organize and establish them. Currently, the district chiefs are quickly organizing and establishing more than seventy townships. It is reported that the county government has already prepared to designate the township chiefs so that they can be formally established. It is expected that it will be fully completed by the end of February.

Village Head Punished for Embezzlement: Xu Naiguang, the village head of Wutu Village, Xiaoshan, was accused by the people of overcharging for land declaration fees last year and was reported to provincial and county agencies, including the county court. After repeated summons and interrogations by the county court, the trial was concluded the other day, sentencing Xu Naiguang to three months in prison and a fine of 200 dollars.

Shangyu 99

Deserters Cause Trouble, Capture Unsuccessful: On the morning of the 15th of this month, the family of Wang Adong, a resident of Yelan Village in Dongxiang, was holding a celebration, and relatives and friends were gathered together when eight deserters carrying rifles and wearing gray military uniforms broke in and caused trouble. Neighbors heard the alarm and sounded the alarm. Seeing that the situation was not good, the deserters fled through the back door of Adong's house and jumped onto a small mountain. Soon, the County Defense Team stationed in Yonghe City and the Salt Patrol Team, after receiving a report from village chief Ye Sanhuai, rushed to surround the mountain occupied by the bandits. After holding out until about 2:00 p.m., the deserters risked charging down the mountainside and fled towards Mojia Lake and Yatang Lake in Yuyao. According to those from Yuyao, when the deserters reached Pingyang, they were all empty-handed, and the firearms they carried were presumably abandoned in the mountains.

Robbery and Kidnapping in Nanhui: The home of Chen Daozheng (also known as Yatou), a resident of Zhaojiali in the Second Community of Nanhui, was broken into on the night of the 18th by more than a dozen bandits wearing long robes and carrying wooden shell guns. They kidnapped his third son (only nine years old) and robbed him of four gold rings, two leather jackets, several pieces of silk and satin, and more than forty silver dollars, resulting in a loss of four to five hundred dollars.

Bengbu 100

Huai River Steamer Robbed: Recently, due to the unrest caused by bandits in northern Anhui, the long-distance Huai River steamships have been robbed from time to time, so passengers are generally wary. The long-distance Tailai steamship, which sailed from Zhengyangguan, was robbed on the 20th. Before it set sail, eight bandits, secretly carrying six Mauser pistols and two steel knives, disguised themselves as merchants and bought tickets to board the ship. The ship loaded passengers and cargo at Zhengyang, set sail with a tow, and sailed downstream. That night, it arrived at Fengtai Wharf and docked. The next morning (21st), it set sail and arrived at Yanke. The bandits suddenly rose up, claiming to be investigating a case, and used their weapons to scare the passengers in the officers' cabins, searching them one by one, robbing them of more than 1,000 dollars in cash. After the robbery, the bandits ordered the ship to dock and went ashore together, fleeing with the stolen goods. After the ship was robbed, it opened to Shitoubu and reported the incident to the local garrison police team. The police led a team to arrest them, but the bandits had already fled without a trace. At 8:00 p.m. that afternoon, when the ship arrived in Yuanyuan, a student named Lu Chuanxue from a school in Tian Shou County returning to Huai was not seen disembarking. His three companions, including Li, searched for him in vain. Yesterday (22nd), they came to Bengbu and asked people to inquire, but there was still no news of him.
