Weather Report 159

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Yangtze River basin and the coast in this area will be cloudy with rain or fog. There is a cyclone here because of a low pressure system in central China, which is moving northeast and east. There are strong northwest winds on the Shandong coast, and east winds south of the Yangtze River estuary. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the local area was 47.2 and the lowest was 30.9. On the same day last year, the highest was 43.5 and the lowest was 31.6.

Letters to the Editor

To the Editor: Having recently read the news column in your January 18th issue, regarding the Zhejiang Construction Department committee taking over the Inland Waterways Merchants' Shipping Bureau, it stated that the accounting staff of the Shanghai-Hangzhou bureaus require more than 10,000 yuan in monthly salaries, resulting in excessive expenses. After investigation, the accounting staff of the Shanghai-Hangzhou bureaus only receive 340 yuan per month, a huge discrepancy from the figure reported in your newspaper. Other reported items, such as the resignation of our bureau chief, are also largely inconsistent with the facts. We hereby request your newspaper to make a correction to avoid spreading false information. We value your professional integrity. Sincerely, Zhejiang Provincial Navigation Administration, January 22nd. To the Editor: Yesterday's article in your esteemed newspaper regarding the cause of Mr. Liu's tragic death contained inaccuracies that do not match the facts. The original article stated that there was a red light as a signal at the south gate, and also said that the gatekeeper was holding a rope, waving a red light, and that the police were assisting in shouting warnings. Even if Mr. Liu was foolish, he would not have been so foolish as to strike a stone with an egg and invite his own demise. It is not known that after Mr. Liu, three sections of fire pump trucks passed through the gate, with no more than three minutes between them. The more than ten firefighters on the trucks did not see any ropes, red lights, or gatekeepers or police calling for them to stop and rescue people. Not only was there no warning or obstruction before the incident, nor police prevention, there were no police, so how could there be shouting? Even five minutes after the incident, they were still asleep. Before and after the incident, they were afraid of the cold and lazy, and neglected prevention to this extent. It is also said that the north gate was being dismantled and repaired by the road engineering office, but it is not known when it was destroyed. Only the railway authorities know about this. Moreover, it was repaired the day after the incident, showing a clear attempt to mend the fold after the sheep are lost. Furthermore, although Mr. Liu's car was knocked dozens of feet away, because the car was small and the cushion was thick, Mr. Liu was only injured on the left side of his face and the corners of his mouth, with no other injuries on his body. It is evident that he lost consciousness due to the violent impact, and then no one came to his rescue, leaving him lying stiff in the icy snow for more than two hours, which is why he died. If it is said that Mr. Liu died from internal injuries, there is a doctor's diagnosis to prove it. Your esteemed newspaper has a duty to record what is heard, but since there are many discrepancies in the facts, we must state the facts and request that they be published in the Letters to the Editor section for correction. Sincerely, The Third Section Fire Brigade of Zhabei, January 23rd.

Important Education News

Military Science Courses Should Be Emphasized 160

The Ministry of Education approved the Directorate General of Training's consultation that military science course hours in senior high schools and above should not be scheduled outside of extracurricular training to emphasize the importance of the subject. A circular was sent to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, stating: "According to a consultation from the Directorate General of Training, 'Lei Zhenzhong, a military instructor in various private secondary schools in Xiamen, reported that the time for military science courses in the schools where he is responsible for military training is mostly scheduled outside of class time. After repeated negotiations, the schools all claim that there is too much coursework and it is impossible to allocate time. Military education is a required course, and if it is implemented outside of class time, most students will be absent, and the practical course will be impossible to implement. It is earnestly requested that a circular be sent to all schools nationwide stating that the time for military science courses must not be scheduled outside of extracurricular training, so as to conform to the main purpose of military education.' Based on this, military education in senior high schools and above has been stipulated as a required course by the plan and the physical education law and cannot be treated the same as optional subjects, causing difficulties in teaching. It is requested that you consult your ministry to issue a circular to all schools, starting from the beginning of the next semester of this year, to promptly correct any of the above situations and emphasize the importance of the subject. We hope to receive a reply." The Ministry of Education has determined that military training is a required subject, as stipulated in the revised military education plan for senior high schools and above, and a circular has been issued stating that students who fail military training will not be allowed to graduate in accordance with Article 6 of the National Physical Education Law. All public and private senior high schools and above should clearly understand the importance of military education, strictly implement training, and strictly prohibit the scheduling of military science course hours outside of extracurricular training, as this violates laws and regulations and disregards military training. In addition to ordering the Fujian Provincial Department of Education to investigate and severely criticize the schools concerned, and ordering them to make corrections, this order is also issued to the "departments" and "bureaus" for them to forward to the senior high schools and above under their jurisdiction for notification.

Survey by the Sino-Belgian Friendship Association

Total of 274 Men and Women

The Sino-Belgian Friendship Association, initiated by Chinese students who have returned from Belgium and Belgian expatriates in China, recently reported that from 1929 to 1930, there were 59 students from Jiangsu, 31 from Zhejiang, 28 from Hebei, 26 from Fujian, 23 from Henan, 22 from Guangdong, 21 from Sichuan, 15 from Hunan, 12 from Hubei, 8 from Yunnan, 6 from Jilin, 5 from Anhui, 4 from Shanxi, and 14 from other provinces, totaling 261 male students and 13 female students, for a total of 274 male and female students. Local News

Another Turmoil at China National College 164

Instruction Stalled, Students Disturbed

(National News Agency) Since the Executive Yuan explicitly ordered the Ministry of Education to investigate China National College President Ma Junwu, all faculty, staff, and students of the college deeply understand that only by urging Ma (Junwu) and Luo (Longji) to leave the college immediately can the student unrest be resolved and the crisis of China National College's demise be eliminated. The details are as follows:

The Office of Academic Affairs Suspended Its Operations. Yesterday (the 23rd), all staff of the Office of Academic Affairs issued a notice, the original text of which reads: "To the Editor: Mr. Ma Junwu violated the resolution of the Board of Directors approving his resignation and refuses to hand over the office. Recently, he has even gone against the tide, excluding dissidents and oppressing them, forcing the Dean of Academic Affairs to resign. We and others, out of love for China National College, have no choice but to temporarily suspend operations in the hope that he will awaken to his senses as soon as possible. We hereby declare. We respectfully hope for your understanding."

The Union to Urge the Assumption of Office. The Union to Resolve Student Unrest, organized by the college students, has reported the details of this dispute to the Ministry of Education, and has telegraphed Minister Jiang to urge Mr. Yu Youren to come to the college as soon as possible to assume the position of president.

The School Protection Association's Advice to Fellow Students. Another group of students in the college has risen up to organize a school protection movement, which many students have endorsed and joined. It is reported that more than three or four hundred people have signed up, and the organization is still in progress today. Yesterday, a letter of advice to fellow students was issued, which stated: "Fellow students, the crisis of China National College has arrived. To enable China National College to overcome this crisis, we can only, at this critical moment, adhere to our conscience, bring out the spirit of unity, adopt reasonable and appropriate measures, and not blindly follow or be deceived by anyone to resolve this danger. (Omitted) Fellow students, the wise students, Mr. Ma has been ordered by the National Government to be investigated. If we do not consider the interests of China National College and the interests of all the students, then we might as well follow the troublesome thugs to make a mess and hold on to China National College for the purpose of destroying it. If we want to take care of the interests of China National College, we should wash our hearts clean, clear our eyes, and use the spirit of concerted effort to tide over the difficulties together to plan for the survival of China National College. Let us no longer wait and see. We recognize this practical phenomenon, aim at this definite goal, and work hard for the survival of China National College and not be used by private individuals. This is our current responsibility. However, with limited abilities, we fear that we will not be able to obtain comprehensive and thorough results in the face of national difficulties. We hope that students will unanimously participate and work together towards the goal of saving the college." In addition, the delegation of representatives of all the students of China National College issued a declaration stating that the issue of changing the president of China National College in Wusong last year caused a great uproar. Then, all the students of the college jointly appealed to the president, Mr. Ma Junwu, to return to the college, which brought peace. At the moment, all the faculty and students of the college are working hard to improve and advance, and the internal stability is as usual. A few people recently secretly organized groups and issued declarations, which were met with an emergency notice published in the newspapers of Shanghai by all the students yesterday (Saturday). Before noon, three or four people posted anonymous notices. The school authorities stopped them, and they reset the students' head portrait, which was obviously injured. The person who was injured reported it to the Seventh District Public Security Bureau and will be prosecuted according to criminal law. At present, the order of the school is maintained by the police sent by the Public Security Bureau, and the situation is very good.

International Soccer Tournament: China Team Mercilessly Beats France 4-0 172

〓Zhou Xianyan's Divine Saves丨Great Goalie, Keeps the Peace Lee Ning and Chen Pu's Great Skills丨No Worries in Our Half of the Field〓

丨Chen Yutian Scores Twice, Chen Hongguang and Xi Qiaosheng Score One Each丨

The sensational International Soccer Tournament is already in its second week of competition. The China team met the France team at Yiyuan yesterday, starting at 3 PM. China put on the pressure from the start but could not find a way to score. The first half ended with no score. In the second half, China scored four goals, setting the final score. From this point on, we will move forward and work hard for the future. Great young men, do not fail in your great mission. The opponent in the second round will be Portugal, who is both tough and skillful. At that time, the Jiannan athletes who conquered the Philippines will be able to serve and fight hard. Although the enemy is strong, we are also elite, and the outcome will depend on the efforts of the warriors.

Young Men Strive for Glory for Their Country Despite Disputes 173

The notice of the China-France match has been posted, and crowds of spectators gathered at Yiyuan. At half past two, the Chinese players, brave and spirited, marched into the field amidst thunderous applause, stretching their legs in the hope of gaining momentum for the battle and winning glory for their country. A group photo of the Chinese and French teams at the International Soccer Tournament (taken by this newspaper)

Clear Difference in Strength, Victory Already in Sight 174

Although the Chinese lineup yesterday was not the strongest or sharpest, it was still far superior to the relatively unknown France team. The difference in strength was obvious, and victory was already in sight. However, in reality, while China had the advantage, France was also good at defending, and each held its own territory securely. Zhou Jiaqi, the secretary of the association, was experienced in battle and insightful into the shortcomings, so he suddenly changed the lineup in the second half, with Chen Hongguang being transferred to center forward and Xi Qiaosheng and Chen Yutian assisting him. Zhou Shaowen was reassigned to right wing. As expected, wherever the army went, the enemy collapsed, and four goals were scored, setting the victory. Zhou Xianyan's performance was amazing, and his save of the twelve-yard penalty was truly a divine save that made people cheer. Li Ning and Guan Xun'an were like impregnable iron walls, difficult for the enemy to breach. Captain Chen Pu took care of both inside and outside defense, and his contribution was great. Veteran Zhu Miao, as a returning player, fought to the end. The amazing work of the five forwards in the first half, although numerous, did not hit the key points, and was not as effective as the flexible and appropriate adaptation in the second half. Chen Yutian opened the scoring, followed by Chen Hongguang, and Chen added another goal, while Xi Qiaosheng ended the game with the final goal. The success of the last three goals was all within ten minutes of the end. French midfielder Selatuo had immense strength and was also commendable. Although the forwards were very agile, their shooting was not skillful, leading to the defeat of the entire army. Referee: Laitai.

A Kick at the Goal, All the Guests Were Startled to Their Feet 175

With three rings of the bell, the clouds of war suddenly spread. The Chinese army, taking advantage of the tailwind, advanced fiercely. It happened that there was a misunderstanding in the passing of the ball by the enemy, so China took the opportunity to enter. Chen Yutian took the lead alone, with a kick at the goal, startling all the guests to their feet. The direction was slightly wrong, and it went diagonally outside the goal. Chen Hongguang went deep alone and hit the goalpost. After China developed twice, the French army launched a combined counterattack, and Chen Pu obstructed from the middle and retreated unfavorably. Chen Hongguang and Xi Qiaosheng shot one after another, first being saved by the goalkeeper, then hitting the wooden post and failing to enter. In short, opportunities for China to shoot were everywhere, but because the field was muddy, it was not easy to kick accurately.

Unity of Effort, Whole and Unbroken Rivers and Mountains 176

The French troops' arrogance suddenly increased; the left wing made frequent contributions; the three central generals were exceptionally flexible; the Chinese front line wavered. Fortunately, Li Ning, Guan Xun, and An were formidable in all directions, guarding key points, resisting the strong enemy. Zhou Xianyan was there to the ball, inseparable, so although the enemy repeatedly attacked, they remained as stable as Mount Tai. Chen Yutian broke through the encirclement in extreme danger, making a solo charge. Subsequently, Chen, with the help of Zhou Shaowen and Xi Qiaosheng, continued to make two more charges. The French troops were fully focused on defense, and nothing happened. In the first half, all parts of the country remained intact.

Breaking Through Enemy Lines, All Rejoice 177

The second half began, and the Chinese team changed its formation. Not long after the kickoff, China and France lunged at each other, with dangerous moments for both sides, but without bloodshed. Ten minutes later, Chen Yutian found an opportunity to advance quickly, kicking the ball towards the goal. The goalkeeper blocked it, but Chen added another kick, breaking through the enemy's defenses. All rejoiced, congratulating Chen Yutian on his success and wishing the Chinese team victory. The enemy looked at each other in dismay, doubling their efforts, but with Zhou Xianyan's great power, they could only sigh at the goal.

Lifting Both Hands, the Iron Gate Remained Intact 178

Chen Yutian tried a long-range shot, and the goalkeeper rushed forward to deflect it. The goal was wide open, and Xi Qiaosheng happened to be there, but unfortunately, he missed to the side. The French center-back dribbled the ball back on the counter-attack, and the ball touched Huang Zhaoguang's arm, resulting in a penalty kick. The French team regained hope, relying entirely on this opportunity, and chose their center forward, Collett, known for his strong and accurate kicks, to take on this important task. However, Zhou Xianyan's eyes were sharp, and his movements were agile. As the ball flew over, he lifted both hands, and the iron gate remained intact. The cheers from the audience were a hundred times louder than before, showing how delighted they were.

River Breaks Its Banks, Falls a Thousand Feet 179

After ten minutes of turbulence, the Chinese team rose again, attacking the fortress three times, lunging at the goal. With a loud bang, the ball broke through the net. The referee ruled that it had touched an enemy's hand first, so the goal was invalid, and a penalty kick was awarded. Chen Hongguang shouldered the hopes of the entire team, raised his foot, and sent the ball towards the goal. The goalkeeper blocked it forward, and Chen Hongguang followed closely, rushing into the net. After the Chinese team scored the second goal, the atmosphere improved greatly. Chen Yutian took advantage of the confusion in the opponent's defense and scored another goal. Not five minutes later, Xi Qiaosheng, in the midst of the crowd, kicked and shot, and also succeeded. The whistle for halftime sounded, and the Chinese team returned in triumph with a score of four to zero.

A Laughing Matter 188

·Sea·Guest

Wife (very gently to her coughing husband): | Darling. You might as well go downstairs to see a new guest. He is waiting for you in the living room.

Husband: | Who is it? Why does he want to see me?

Wife: | You must forgive me for this. I went to invite him. But lately you have been coughing so much. I am very worried. What if I lose you?

Husband (smiling): | My love. I just caught a chill and have a slight cough. Would I really die? Why are you so alarmed? Please call a doctor for me.

Wife: | Not a doctor. A salesman from a life insurance company.

A: | Friend. I advise you to take a break. Why are you writing day and night?

B: | I am writing a novel. There is a lot of profit to be made in this.

A: | Don't fool people. I can buy a thick novel for just a few cents. What great profit is there to be made? Is it worth it for you to pour out your heart and blood for a few cents?

Customer: | How many years have you been running this grocery store?

Owner: | Three years now.

Customer: | I see you have many customers. Your business must be good.

Owner: | Business is good, but I am too busy.

Customer: | I see that lady has to greet customers and manage accounts. It is really hard work.

Owner: | She is my wife. It would be best if I had two more like her.

A Record of the German Aviation Technology Performance 189

Dawei

After the German Swiss Lieshi flew a Junkers aircraft to Beijing, he tried out his skills. The movements were dangerous, and the viewers were terrified. On the 20th of the month, because Chairman Jiang had to come to observe in person, a second performance was made. That afternoon, the sky was gloomy, and the north wind howled. At about 4 pm, Chairman Jiang arrived at the Ming Palace Airfield. Director of the Aviation Department Zhang Huichang and Deputy Director Huang Bingheng had already been waiting at the airport to welcome him. He introduced the German Swiss Lieshi to Chairman Jiang to shake hands and meet. Both smiled happily. Swiss was strong and energetic, carrying an insurance umbrella and wearing thick leather flying clothes. The buttons were tightly fastened and all made of metal. After meeting, he jumped into the plane. The engine started, and he rose straight up like an arrow. After flying around once, he went straight into the clouds. He completely shut down the engine. There was no sound. He dived down, very close to the ground. He then resumed level flight. He then made a small turn of ninety degrees. He then rose again and spiraled down. He then continued to turn circles, making a small Yinmeimeng-style turn. He rose again and inverted the plane, making the wheels face up and the person upside down. He was able to maintain this for six or seven minutes. He was able to continue moving forward and make several small turns. The viewers all changed color, but he safely returned to his original state. He also performed slow flight, like a turtle. According to aviators, it is difficult to make a large aircraft with less horsepower move slowly. It is like a bicycle. To ride slowly, you must be experienced. The plane is also like this. In addition, he performed rolling flight, inverted flight, sideslip, and inverted roll one by one, and was able to fly silently in the air for more than ten minutes. High-altitude flight

Inviting Guests to Jiaoshan to Watch the Moon at its Peak, I Was Unable to Go, and Yiru and Mo Jun Went Instead, Both Showed Me What They Had Made, and I Answered with This Poem 190

— Hu Zhantang

How many pairs of clogs do I wear in a lifetime? How many times do I see the moon at its peak in a lifetime? Both are optimistic and good at words. The former is praised, and the latter is diminished. In those years, crossing the river transformed into a dragon. After the Jin and Song dynasties, Wang Jiangdong. I do not see the black iron cavalry of the Yaer, but ask about the swallows and spring lanterns. With a cup in hand, things are already sufficient. Looking in the mirror, I turn to face the picture of the beautiful one. The Han family's three hundred professions are cut in half. Thus, the mediocre lord is guilty. My friend Mao Sheng does not think so. He says that this judgment is unfair. What fault does the emperor have in his romantic affairs? No official first cried for the Ming Emperor Sizong. The old treacherous officials Ma and Ruan really misled the country. Moreover, the Hu fortune was not a human achievement. Do you not see the copper platform where the fragrance of the courtesans is thin? At the Bai Liang banquet, the concubines vied to bite the red dates. Who knows that deep drinking is not a wild banquet? It is often not in the Xianyang Palace. Do you also not see the pitiful sons of the Six Dynasties emperors? The Five Dynasties are all scoundrels who became heroes. Holding to the success or failure of this and dismissing that, the difference between Zang and Gu is like Zhuang Meng. Let me ask you about the moon above your head. Who can follow those who treat all things as discarded shoes? Therefore, I invite you to the Golden Jiao Peak. The good festival also has good companions meeting. Shao's couple Guang and Hong. I do not know if Xu is pursuing the poor. Waiting for the moon and getting rain will be no different. Returning, they all sing with a long wind. I have clogs, but I am too lazy to wax them.

Finished. He then performed low-altitude flight, no more than tens of feet from the airfield, circling, flying inverted, and undulating, skimming over the heads of the audience. When descending, he went straight to the aircraft hangar, and everyone thought that he would touch the top of the hangar and cause a major disaster. It was almost unbearable to look at. Who knew that as he approached the hangar, he slightly raised his head and landed safely. Alas, his skills are truly miraculous. In short, no matter what high-level flying action, he felt comfortable and handy. A huge plane, to him, was like a light withered leaf. He played with it arbitrarily without falling. On this day, everyone who watched sighed at his superb skills. Even Chairman Jiang frequently nodded in approval. It is a pity that this performance was not announced in advance. Apart from the aviation industry, most people were unaware of it. Even the newspapers rarely recorded it, so I wrote a note about it.

A Trip to Tangshan 191

— Jiang Meisheng

Dai Jun Zhiang is studying at Central University. He is kind to my daughter and husband Xu Beihong. On January 18th of the 20th year of the Republic, Dai Jun came by motorcycle and invited us to Tangshan for a trip. Everyone was happy and followed him. Those who went with him were French professor Shao Kelu, Dai Jun's friend Ding Jun, my second daughter Biwei, and grandson Boyang. The young and old totaled seven people. Tangshan is about fifty miles away from Xindu. The motorcycle can reach it in one hour. On that day, we started at 10:30 am and did not arrive until 1:30 pm because we were delayed along the way.

Earlier, Beihong had once gone to Qinglong Mountain, where he said there was a huge stele material, carved from a stone cliff, and one end was not different. It stood sideways on the ground, approximately sixty feet long (or wide), fourteen meters high (or wide), and four meters thick. It is truly a spectacle in the universe. According to historical research, in the Yongle dynasty of the Ming dynasty, it was planned to be used to engrave a stele of sacred virtue and divine merit. Afterwards, it did not succeed and was abandoned in the wilderness. Everyone who heard this was moved and wanted to explore its wonder. On that day, they parked the car in the village and walked to find it. Unexpectedly, it was far away. The rice paddies were muddy and slippery, and there were many thorns on the mountain path. I was particularly afraid to walk, so I stopped in the middle of the road, waiting for my companions to return and descend together. So I sat alone on a rock for more than an hour. Looking around, there was no one. There was only desolate grass and cold wind, solemn and piercing the skin to the bone. Fortunately, it was noon. If it were dusk, even the heart of Meng Ben would probably tremble with fear. After a long time, my companions finally arrived. Then we followed the path down the mountain, got into the car, and continued on. In less than twenty minutes, Tangshan was reached.

The mountain is named after the hot springs. In the past, it was covered with weeds and unknown to the world. It only became slightly famous since the Republic of China. As Xindu was being built, it became a scenic area. The Tangshan Club was organized by four giants, members of the National Government, etc., to provide rest and recreation during their political leisure. Outsiders were not allowed to enter. There are facilities to sell bath water for the public to bathe in, with varying levels of quality. The best is called Taolu, where you can eat and bathe. The price is slightly higher. Those with middle-class income or above often go there. When we arrived, we also entered. We were planning to order wine and choose dishes to fill our hungry stomachs, but a certain gentleman in charge of the club insisted on inviting Dai Jun, saying, "There are no guests in the club today. Since the young master has graced us with his presence, it is appropriate to entertain guests there. Don't be humble." So Dai Jun led the guests into the club and ordered lunch, a total of nine dishes. The taste was very delicious. After eating, we were invited to bathe. The place where I bathed was almost the residence of a certain giant. The carpet was soft and thick, and there were brocade couches and copper beds, almost like a first-class room in a large hotel. Inside, there was a bath pool. The pool was paved with cement and was rectangular, more than a丈long and three-fifths wide. The spring was also opened and closed with a manually operated machine, like an ordinary bathhouse, but cleaner. The temperature was suitable, and the bath was pleasant. Everyone bathed one by one. It was already early evening. We then walked to the Tangwang Temple, two miles away. The temple was narrow and unworthy of seeing, but there was a peony tree behind the hall. The branches and trunks were lush and thick, almost a hundred years old. It is a pity that we did not see the prosperous state of its flowers in bloom. To the west of the temple, there is also a hot spring pool, surrounded by short walls, with walls dividing it to separate men and women. Farmers and workers bathed there. Compared to the club, I could not help but sigh and say that the realization of equality is not easy. So we returned to the club, got into the car, and started on our way home. Before leaving, Beihong took out five coins to reward the soldiers who served us, but the gentleman in charge refused to accept it. This is enough to show the strict training of the principal, and we were really sorry. When we turned the wheels and drove quickly into the city, the city was already full of lights.

Night-Shining Wood 192

— Yan Jun

Yesterday I visited Mr. Someone who was ill. I saw a copy of his draft work, Moving Bricks, on his desk. I borrowed it to take home. In it, there were two poems about night-shining wood, along with a preface. It is a very unusual thing. I am transcribing it for Free Talk for the study of botanists. The preface said, "When I first moved the ancestral shrine, there were four cypress trees planted. Three were flourishing, but one on the west side had been repeatedly replaced because it was dying. Last year, it was replanted again. The withered stump was removed and discarded. After more than a month, when the bark was peeled off, it suddenly glowed at night. The roots were especially bright white. My clan son Kui Jiu said, 'This is probably what is called night-shining wood.' We treasured it and stored it away carefully. In the Kangxi dynasty, night-shining wood was obtained, and the Sacred Ancestor had an imperial edict about it, which still shines in the literary world today. Later, Mr. Hua Yundi of our town, my paternal aunt's husband, was fond of Taoism in his later years. In the year of Bing Shen in the Qianlong era, he obtained night-shining wood. For a time, celebrities wrote poems and eulogies about it, almost everywhere. It was bound into four volumes, crowned with a small portrait. I read it over and over again, appreciating its jewels, and always regretted not seeing this wood. Now it has actually been produced on the site of our family's ancestral shrine, emitting the faint light of potential virtue, to magnify our clan. Is this the beginning of the omen? Therefore, I composed two poems to commemorate it." The poem said, "It is said that the luminous pearl is a rare treasure in the world. Is it not laborious to turn the mound to find it? Who knows that in the depths of the night, a foot-long piece of wood shines like a god at my door? It is said that wherever it is passed around, darkness turns to light. Everyone is surprised that it has been obtained in the human world." "I broke off a branch and carried it to Suzhou City, showing it to everyone. In the end, no one recognized it." Perhaps the star spirit pities those who read at night, so it blows the reed fire to be a lamp for books. "Moving Bricks" still exists. The author's name is not given below. It was written by someone with the surname Huang from Wuxi. Mr. Someone said,

Parisian Tales (10) (3) 193

6. Once Resided in Paris

Since the invention of sound film, people have predicted that there would be no more stage plays besides movies. Since movies can speak and sing, anything that stage plays can do, movies can also do. But movies can do things that stage plays cannot. "Donogoo" was adapted from a movie script and required a total of 27 scenes and sets. This is rare in stage plays. Only the large mechanical stage of the Pigalle Theatre can perform it. The performance of "Donogoo" is intended to expand the scope of stage play sets to compete with movies. Therefore, some say that the future of stage plays can be predicted from the success or failure of the play "Donogoo".

The content of "Donogoo" is roughly as follows: a man named Lamendin stands on a bridge over a river, preparing to commit suicide. A friend happens to pass by and saves him, introducing him to a psychiatrist for treatment. The doctor's prescription is to have him stand in front of the Paris Mosque at 5:45, approach the first person who passes by him wiping their nose, and dedicate his whole body and mind to that person. Lamendin follows the doctor's instructions and indeed sees the first person wiping their nose passing by at that place and time. This is Professor Yves le Tronhadec. Lamendin strikes up a conversation with the professor and follows him home. The professor tells him the thing he most hopes for: to be elected as a member of a national academy. With his qualifications as a professor, this should be quite possible. But unfortunately, he wrote in a world geography book about a city that doesn't exist. This city is purely fictional. To remedy this mistake, the non-existent city must be created. Lamendin resolutely accepts this task. He is going to create the city of Donogoo, which does not actually exist. The most complicated part of the play begins here.

Warmth in the Heart (3)(5)(6) 194

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 17: Techniques to Preserve Youthful Looks, Faded Eyebrows, No Way to Prolong Life, a Golden Market for Fine Horses

Ren Peizhen said, "What they especially mess up themselves is using religion to deceive the people, using foolish tricks to cheat people, saying that after practicing that kind of boxing, they will be invulnerable to knives and spears. Indeed, in the past, in martial arts, they practiced a kind of 'toad strength,' where a knife would only leave a white mark when it cut. But now, tactics don't use those weapons anymore. Can you dodge bullets one by one? If you practiced martial arts that could not be penetrated by bullets, that would be a great invention. The world wouldn't need to talk about science anymore, and the country wouldn't need to run any military factories. It's a pity that those foolish people were fooled by them. It wasn't until the Allied forces entered and they died in rows from bullets that they realized, but it was already too late." Old Lin Daiyu said, "It's a little strange. I saw them recite incantations, make a strong posture, and be bare-chested. The muscles all over their bodies swelled up, and they used a big knife to chop down on their arms, but there wasn't a single scratch. A person is made of flesh and blood, not wrapped in copper and iron. Although it is said that northerners are tough guys, they never shout or beg for mercy when a knife goes in and blood comes out, but it's not easy to develop that kind of strength." Zuo Shichen said, "When we were seven or eight years old, we visited Yuanmiao Temple in Suzhou. There were many people selling their boxing skills inside. We also saw them practice that kind of toad strength. When they burst their energy, knives couldn't cut them. When we saw it at first, we also thought it was a bit strange. With our childish minds, we thought it must be a dull knife. Otherwise, if you practice this strength, even if you chop your head, you wouldn't be able to chop it off. There's no way that's true. Probably those Boxers were using these people who sold their boxing skills to create a sense of mystery and incite a group of ignorant people with their childish knowledge. I heard that they also set up an altar and worshiped some ancestral masters, teaching everyone to worship. Therefore, there were names like 'Senior Brother' and 'Second Senior Brother.' They also used the names of heroes from novels. I know that recently, books like *The Cases of Magistrate Shi*, *The Cases of Peng Gong*, and *Seven Heroes and Five Gallants* have been selling a lot in the north. After reading those books, everyone wants to be a hero. And after seeing plays, young people all want to be Huang Tianba. Unconsciously, it has deeply influenced people's hearts. With a little incitement, they cause trouble." Old Lin Daiyu said, "I've been to the altar they set up. It was in Zhuang Yu's mansion. Inside, there were yellow curtains, yellow carpets, and yellow candles. It was extraordinarily solemn. People who drink and eat meat are not allowed to step inside. Many princes and ministers went inside devoutly to kowtow and burn incense. After they caught the 'foreign devils,' they would come to the altar to present a memorial. If the memorial could be raised, the ancestral master would indicate that they were good people. If the memorial could not be raised, the ancestral master would indicate that they were bad people and they would be taken out and beheaded. When the memorials were being raised, everyone looked pale and trembled."

Total daily transactions were 147,000 dan. Sold out Shenda 5,700 dan, Gengfeng 3,100 dan, Gongtai 8,800 dan, Yiyu 3,900 dan, and Minghua 3,300 dan. American cotton prices showed mixed trends, with near-term contracts rising and distant contracts falling. Last Week's American Cotton Sales Were Very Good 203

A dispatch from New York on the 23rd reported on raw cotton for the week: The cotton market showed a slight downward trend at the beginning of the week, but was soon halted by increased demand from peers. A portion of this was due to increased orders for Japanese cotton cloth due to the Lancashire mill strike. There was also buying in Europe and domestically, which led to new short positions covering their positions. They were wary of the market remaining so firm despite weak current demand. During the price increase, Southern supplies showed a slight improvement, but all sales were absorbed. The Lancashire labor unrest is unresolved, and the Liverpool market remains stable. Egyptian cotton is also firm, which is also a reason for optimism. The price difference between New York and Liverpool is currently quite large. It seems that the overall trend will readjust the price difference in the global market, or it may be a sign of possible export demand in the spring and summer seasons. However, the demand for inventory replenishment in various countries is not currently urgent. Attachment: Statistics as follows, in thousands of bales.

Grain and Rice Market Prices in Hexia Increase Sharply 205

Ordinary Grades Fall Again by 20 Cents

Yesterday, the arrival of river boats in Zhabei was still strong, with over 70 boats arriving. The reason for the recent surge is that they were previously affected by wind and snow and were delayed en route. Currently, various inland waterways have gradually become clear, so the accumulated rice boats have arrived simultaneously. Therefore, the source of these later arrivals may decrease. Sales by various guilds in the market yesterday were still sluggish. Genuine high-grade japonica rice was scarce, so it remained on the left side of the 14 yuan mark, while ordinary grades fell again by 20 cents. The situation will depend on the weather. If it turns cloudy, then it may be able to stand firm for a day or two. Indica rice has suffered a setback, and the market has also fallen slightly. Sheep indica rice is indeed scarce, so although sales are sluggish, prices remain flat. Du indica rice lacked buying interest in both the port and pointed grades, and prices were set high with subsequent cuts. Specially variable yuan rice was selling well, with prices requiring 13 yuan 78 cents, while secondary grades required a cut of more than 10 cents. With both shaded and transformed arrivals seeing slow sales, the market presented a fluctuating picture. Throughout the day, various conditions have shifted to an increased trend of price cuts.

Yesterday, over 30 rice boats arrived in Shanghai South, with sales lacking. Common guild large market white japonica rice was wholesaled for 15 cents. Top-grade goods were being given away, and the market was flat. Suzhou former white japonica retail sales were extremely sluggish, and with ample river storage, they became increasingly depressed, falling by 10 to 20 cents each. The trend of indica rice from various locations in the South Road became increasingly weak, with a total drop of 50 cents in recent days. Currently, the special high-grade indica rice is only opening at 11 yuan. Although the sources of sheep and Du pointed grade rice were received, the bottom-grade goods were depleted, so the market was still able to maintain the original price. Variable shaded yuan rice was sluggish and lifeless, with top-grade goods in the market appearing stable, and medium-grade unified repairs being just left of 10 cents.

Further Shipments of Guangdong Rice from Jiangxi 206

Yesterday, the market conditions for guest indica rice showed that the source of Jiangxi rice was relatively scarce, and the local appetite was very sluggish. Although there were inquiries from the guest guild, market prices had already softened by several cents. Only Hunan rice and Nanjing rice had low arrivals and storage, so the market was still able to stand firm. Yesterday, the Guangdong guild's appetite was still good, purchasing over 2,000 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled late rice, with prices slightly softer, selling at 11 yuan 57 cents to 11 yuan 20 cents. The Ningbo guild purchased 220 bags of Hunan red rice at a price of 10 yuan 01 cent. The local street only purchased over 400 bags of brown rice, with Nanjing brown rice at 8 yuan 50 cents to 8 yuan 45 cents, and Willow brown rice at 8 yuan 80 cents. There were no other transactions reported.

The Flour Market Continues to Show Signs of Slackness 207

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, all months showed signs of fatigue. With the quotation for foreign wheat falling by another 10 to 20 cents, people's minds were already softening. In the afternoon, it was further rumored that foreign firms were again offering foreign wheat to factories and dealers. According to private sources, Australian white wheat was again shouting down to Shen yuan 4 taels, or it was rumored that Fuxin's order was only 3 taels 9 qian and 5 fen (handled by Mitsui and Longmao), totaling around 20,000 tons. Therefore, short sellers in the market were actively moving, and factories were also enthusiastically hedging. With foreign wheat arriving one after another, it is finally difficult to see a turnaround in the market in the future. As a result, this month was down 1 cent from the previous day, February was down 7.5 li, and March to June were each down 1.5 cents.

The Fall in Forward Wheat Prices is Particularly Severe 208

Yesterday, after the opening of the forward wheat market in the morning and afternoon, each month presented a picture of initial firmness followed by a decline. Although the quotation for foreign wheat fell in the morning, short sellers took the opportunity to enter, so it did not fall but instead improved. January and February were better by 1 to 2 cents than the previous day. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, the price of the continued foreign wheat order was cheaper, and the quantity was better. Those belonging to the dealer naturally offered it to the market, causing the forward months to decline like a river, without looking back. According to this kind of scene, the forward standard may have to pass through the 4 tael mark before there is a day of return. As a result, this month fell 2 cents from the previous day, February fell 3 cents, March, April and May each fell 5 cents, and June fell 4 cents. There has been no trading of spot wheat due to factory inaction.

The Rising Trend of Standard Soybeans Turns Fierce 209

Future Bean Cakes Slightly Followed Suit

Yesterday, the standard soybean market was selling well. The morning opening market was only slightly good. Later, due to the fact that various guilds had to cover their recent holdings, the situation gradually tightened. At the afternoon opening, dealers and the Great Dalian Private Telegram reported high prices, and customers from Lianbang frequently inquired. Each month's futures market was gradually firm. This month, due to the upcoming delivery, spot soybeans were selling extremely well, and arrivals were slightly stable, so people's minds improved. Therefore, near-term buying interest turned strong, and the rising trend became fierce. Although a small number of guest guilds sold off the distant months, they also followed the upward trend. At the close, January futures were up 7 cents, February futures were up 5 cents, March futures were up 4 cents, and April and May were each up 2 cents.

The futures bean cake market initially felt firm, and then there was inland support, which was quickly secured. Continued to rise due to rising raw materials and reports of Lianxun's high prices, but there were not many transactions in the morning and afternoon sessions, so the market only showed signs. As a result, February and June each rose by 1 cent, April rose by 1 cent and 2 li, and May rose by 7 li and 5 hao.

Prices for Northern and Southern Goods and Glutinous Rice Branches Slightly Slacken 210

Glutinous rice branches have seen a slight easing in market prices in recent days due to a decline in sales. Inquiries have shown that dealers still have stock, and there are also shipments arriving. The former price for Chung Chong goods was 84 to 85 taels, now it is 82 to 83 taels, a decrease of 2 to 3 taels from before. There has been little trading in the inland areas of the local street recently. The former price for high-grade goods was 90 taels, but it has also decreased.

Silk and Tea, European and American Silk Sales Remain Strong 211

Yesterday, the local Shanghai foreign firm silk market remained strong. It was found that overseas silk telegrams for both yellow and white silk had been transferred to Shanghai, and various manufacturers were very reluctant to sell due to insufficient inventory. Yesterday, Jardine Matheson etc. imported 20 packages of Shanghai white factory silk, Sinfu imported 10 packages of Lu yellow factory silk, and Mei Da imported 8 packages of coarse yellow silk, with prices all firm.

Over 70 Cases of Tin Factory Silk Were Transported to Shanghai 212

In Preparation for Delivery to Foreign Firms at the End of the Month

Various silk factories in Wuxi have undertaken to throw this month's futures silk. Because the end of the month is approaching, they are actively reeling silk and transporting it to Shanghai in batches in preparation for delivery to foreign firms. Yesterday, a Shanghai-Wuxi passenger train again loaded 75 cases of white factory silk, all of which were picked up by various Shanghai silk brokers to be delivered.

Piece Goods and Foreign Red Labels See a Sharp Increase 213

The trend of local factory cloth was slightly soft yesterday, probably because the Lunar New Year is approaching, and local customers are showing a closing trend, so sales have slowed. All goods that are mortgaged with silver are willing to sell, resulting in fine cloth first falling by about 5 cents yesterday. Yanghe, Caiqiu, and Laba Tong were all 6 taels 9 qian and 5 fen, blue Double Fish was 7 taels and 5 fen, 11-pound blue Sun was 6 taels 5 qian, and 12-pound blue Chicken was 6 taels 8 qian and 2.5 fen. Fine twill was also slightly down, with Yanghe at 7 taels 3 qian and 2.5 fen, and blue Double Fish at 7 taels. However, 9-pound coarse cloth continued to rise, actually because of a lack of spot goods. Yesterday, Five Bats reached 4 taels 4 qian and 5 fen, Cat Owl was 4 taels 4 qian and 2.5 fen, 11-pound goods remained flat, 13-pound Double Eagle opened at 6 taels, coarse twill was quite stiff, Two Fish sold for 5 taels 4 qian, Three Rabbit was 5 taels 3 qian and 7.5 fen, and Cat Owl had no goods.

Eastern and Western piece goods saw more declines than increases, actually because the date of total closing is not far away. The local street was already very quiet yesterday, and customers' searches were also slow, so people's minds were softening. Yesterday, the black flower, water wave, and bleached flannel of the Eastern goods all fell, each by a small 2.5 li. The concubine color cotton and French flannel of Yijianjian also gradually fell. Yesterday, Yang Guifei color was 2 qian and 2 fen, Wumeiren red was 2 qian and 2.5 fen. Fine serge was softer with the Sanyou Tu of Tu Yuan, opening at 3 qian and 1.5 fen, and the rest remained firm. Spot tribute cloth was still lacking, and foreign red labels actually increased. Yesterday, it opened at a new high price never seen before, with 6-pound Guo Ju at 4 taels 9 qian and 5 fen, Santan Yin Yue Qiao at 4 taels 8 qian and 5 fen, and 4-pound Guo Ju reaching 4 taels 2 qian and 5 fen. Changing the brand also required 4 taels to pass through customs.

The Oil Market, Tung Oil Continues to Rise 214

Since the price of white tung oil soared, the Hong and Xiu oils, which are suitable for production areas, are just at the time of closing and starting crushing. The fundamental impact of the futures market is inevitable. It is obvious that the future cost will inevitably be high. However, since the autumn, Xiu oil has arrived in one batch, and there has been no source for a long time. When it arrived, it happened to be at the time when white tung oil plummeted, so it has repeatedly fallen in price. Sanxiu, comprising Zhongwei, Wanxingyu, and Dayouheng, has fallen from 29 taels and 6 qian to 25 taels, a total of 4,000 to 5,000 pieces, which have been sold as prices have fallen. Therefore, there are only a few hundred pieces left in the local area. It is reported that Jifengheng and Jitaiheng have recently arrived in Hankou with 2,000 to 3,000 pieces. According to the voices of the purchasing customers, Jifengheng must sell for 30 taels, and Jitaiheng must sell for 28 taels, both of which are flourishing. If this is compared to the recent decline in the Shanghai market, it must be increased by one or two taels. The various dealers are unwilling to increase prices because the goods have already been sold, so naturally, those with goods in hand must increase prices and sell if they encounter a buyer. After the addition of Hongjiang oil, inland areas have sold a lot before the establishment of unified taxes. The price of Qingyuanfeng and Fuhong from 1919 is 19 taels 6 qian, and the goods from 1918 can be reduced by 2 to 3 taels. The same brand has such a large price difference due to the year, which is also a novel phenomenon. Yang Hengyuan's Fuhong requires 19 taels and 8 qian, and other brands have varying prices. The approximate range is from 19 taels to 18 taels and a few cents, while Xiang Taifeng and Jifengying have the lowest price of 21 taels, and there are not many goods. Yesterday, the market repeatedly increased the price of white tung oil, so various ports in Beijing increased the price by 6 qian. It is said that it will need to be increased again.

Miscellaneous: 30,000 bags of Wuhu white rice will be shipped to Guangzhou immediately. 860 cases of French foreign wine arrived yesterday. 240 cases of woolen fabrics and silk fabrics arrived from Paris. 6,200 bags of East Sugar have been imported. 160 cases of paint came from England. 1.3 million feet of lumber came from America. 970 pieces of iron wire were shipped from Europe. 460 pieces of machinery came from London. 1,000 pieces of glass came from Dalian. 3,600 boxes of tea were loaded in Hankou.

Shanghai Market

Theater News 215

The Universal Theater announced that it will begin screening today the recently produced two-part Shi Gong An: The Tale of the Zither and Xiao by Tianyi Film Company. This film depicts the ultimate in eroticism and warmth, and is one of the most idyllic pages in the Shi Gong An novel. The theater will screen the scene of climbing the wall to flirt, playing the zither and xiao in harmony, which is accompanied by the sounds of master musicians playing the instruments live. It is practically a sound-and-music film scene.

The Lone Star Film Company announced that its original studio on Dixwell Road was insufficient, so it has moved to 505 Jiangwan Road and built two new large studios, equipped with dozens of the latest lighting fixtures, and is working day and night without sparing any effort. Recently, the company filmed The Legend of Jin Tai. Although this book is a work of gods and monsters, the characters written about have the spirit of loyalty and righteousness. The company did not hesitate to spend a lot of money to film this film, because the chivalrous spirit in the book is very admirable. The company has been preparing for this drama for a year, seeking the exquisite production of the production. It is produced by Huang Wenjun, directed by Lu Yeyuan, and stars Qian Siying, Bao Gusong, He Huijuan, Chen Yanfang, Tang Xueqian, Wu Yixiao, Zi Chun, and others. Director Lu will lead all the actors to take exterior shots around Taihu Lake this Wednesday.

The Plum Blossom Girl Song and Dance Troupe announced that they have returned from Hangzhou and have signed a contract with the Central Theater to perform for three days starting on the 31st. This program includes the latest rewritten ideal opera, Not Seeing Last Year's Person. The material for this play is based on the Japanese Nomura collection of poetry, Lan Niang's Return, which is a supremely sensual and poignant ideal work. At this time of the new rise of Chinese song and dance, this play can be called the epoch-making work of Chinese song and dance in 1931.

The Shanxi Grand Theater announced that, in order to increase the interest of customers, they have specially invited the Qunhua Girl Song and Dance Troupe to perform. Among them, Ms. Fu Wenying, the flower of song and dance, has the best voice and dance. The stage has been full every day. Yesterday was the last day, with special treatment, day and night performances of the funny and delicate song and dance drama Little Painter, and at the same time screening the brave warrior and the good film of the foreign country starring the martial arts star Ding Mike. The price is the same as before. The troupe has accepted invitations from Tongzhou, Xiamen, and other places, and will leave Shanghai soon.

Medical News 216

Chinese medicine practitioner Feng Peijun announced that he specializes in gynecology, pediatrics, and internal and surgical medicine. Due to his increasingly busy practice, the original Jiangyuan Nong clinic was insufficient, so he specially moved to Jishanli at the intersection of Jiangyuan Nong East and Wenzhou Road yesterday, and is open as usual.

The China Harmonica Association announced that after the association's first broadcast on Asia-America Company, it was praised by people from all walks of life. There have been several letters requesting another broadcast. This association will broadcast at the invitation of Tianling Company Radio Station on the 24th. The program is as follows: (1) Harmonica ensemble Nostalgia Overture, ... China Harmonica Team, (2) Duet Double-Headed Eagle March, ... Ke Hongsui, Qin Jianqing, (3) Qin ensemble American Patrol, ... Wang Qingxun, Liu Yin, (7) Harmonica solo Student Army March, ... Wang Qingxun, (8) Harmonica ensemble Heart of a Prostitute, ... China Harmonica Team. The Bilu Chinese Correspondence School announced that Bilu Zou Zhanruqun is a senior in Huai'an, a high-ranking disciple of the poet Duan Hutlin, and is very proficient in classical Chinese prose and poetry. Chen Shiyi, a Houguan official, had already selected and included Zou's work in his collection of poetry. The school has now been established at No. 13 Anli, on the west side of the French Concession in Shanghai. It specializes in modifying and answering questions. Its wit and brilliance surpass others and is truly rare at present. Scholars near and far who study the essence of the country all send their greetings by post.

The Nanjing Road National Products Department Store announced that the factory will hold a large-scale cotton textile sale starting yesterday. Yesterday was the first day of the sale. From morning to night, customers came in an endless stream. The prosperity of the business was unprecedented. All kinds of cotton textiles produced by various Chinese factories, such as bed sheets, pillowcases, bathrobes, and towels, numbering no less than dozens of varieties, are displayed in the department store's own business department. According to buyers, the quality is not inferior to that of imported goods, and the price is much lower. The newly invented pocket stove is ingenious, small, light, and extremely beautiful, so buyers are also very enthusiastic. The amusement park at the east end of the department store performs comedy and new-style songs and dances and other various amusements day and night. Anyone who buys goods for more than one yuan will receive a beauty photo and an amusement ticket.
